--- 帖子 #1 ---
Before you run the EAs, read my FAQ: http://www.forexfactory.com/showthread.php?t=252690

Read http://www.forexfactory.com/showthread.php?t=251869

to get an idea of what this kind of strategy is all about.

This strategy intentionally trims the biggest loser and opens an opposite-direction trade on the same pair whenever at least three losing pairs have breached their 24-hour high/low.

The way this is done is quite restrained, such that overtrimming is avoided. We want to do just enough trimming that we allow the same market action that triggered the trimming to take us to profit.

So do not be alarmed when the first actions taken by the EA make your balance shrink. If you are patient, a rise in equity will occur and all trades will be closed for profit.

There are old-school elements to this strategy, such as diversification (14 pairs), cut your losses early (cut the BIGGEST loser when market action makes it a logical decision), and let your winners run (until you come into profit).

Basket_14 was developed before Confirm_14. Basket_14 uses less specific criteria in looking for confirmation. It looks for a total of 3 currency pairs among the 14 to be breaching their 24-hour highs/lows before trimming and reversing a biggest loser.

Attach to only one chart, any symbol, any timeframe. Don't worry about opening other charts. You only need to open ONE.

Version 02 does not have the MinMiniEquity and MinStdEquity settings.

Version 03 uses two seven-pair relative vigor index (RVI) indicators to try to increase the frequency with which we get to profit without trimming and reversing.

Version 04 looks for five samples of RVI main to be above/below zero, cleanly separated across the two groups of seven pairs, to decide which group to buy/sell.

Version 05 has buy/sell logic based on RVI main/signal crosses above/below zero

Settings for Various Leverage Levels

Leave the settings as-is for a 200:1 leverage account.

Set MaxMarginToUse to 2.0 for a 100:1 leverage account and leave ProfitPct at 1.0.

Set MaxMarginToUse to 3.0 and ProfitPct to 0.3 for a 10:1 leverage account. This may seem risky but most of us will want to push risk if we get restricted to 10:1 accounts. Even with this risk level, you shouldn't see Lowest Margin drop much below 200%.

For my 50:1 demo, I am using MaxMarginToUse at 3.0 and ProfitPct at 0.75. So far it's working fine.

--- 帖子 #20 ---
A nice thing is that sometimes we get into profit without any trim'n'reverse actions.

That might seem odd because the two groups of seven pairs represent a perfect synthetic hedge. But across this many pairs, distortions do happen as all pairs can move independently.

So I just uploaded version 03, which uses two seven-pair relative vigor index (RVI) indicators to try to increase the frequency with which we get to profit without trimming and reversing. No guarantee that we won't have to trim and reverse with this approach, but at least we tip the odds a little in that direction.

How it works is: the group of 7 that shows the stronger RVI is the group that we will sell, and we will buy the other.

It shouldn't matter which group we initially buy or sell, as long as we always buy one group and sell the other. However, since there are observable imbalances at times, we might as well attempt to find which side to be on if in fact it could make any difference at all.

The nice thing is -- the cut'n'reverse scheme is stable and has proven time and time again to nudge the basket toward profit, even though it sometimes takes some patience to get some wind in the sails via strong market action.  This element alone will get us to profit regardless of which side is bought vs sold.  It's just that we want to get our profit faster if possible.  Nothing wrong with that, is there?

--- 帖子 #25 ---
Hello sky... It is not necessary to close MetaCoder's EAs manually. There is always a user setting that allows you to have the EA automatically stop trading after taking profit. Just set StopAfterNoTrades to true. When the EA closes all trades for the 1% profit it will stop trading. When you are ready to start trading again, go back in and change it back to false and it will immediately open the 14 trades again. COOL

There is virtually nothing that needs to be done manually when using MetaCoder's EAs.

--- 帖子 #36 ---
The ProfitTarget setting is a percentage of LastFlatEquity. Your screen comments show that your current Equity is 30771 and your Equity Profit Target is 30797 ($5 above your LastFlatEquity which was 30787). The trades will be closed when Equity reaches 30797 - 26 more $s. This EA will never close all trades based on PL and it will never close all trades for a loss. It is looking for a profit above LastFlatEquity (Equity at time of last close all). Everything is based on equity.

Also, you need to understand that, except for a close all, the EA only closes losing trades and will never close just 1 winner. For that reason, we never try to calculate how much the EA is making or losing until we get a close all.

There are always 14 open trades with this EA. Every time it trims a loser it reopens that pair in the opposite direction. It takes profit by closing all trades when the Profit Target is reached. Then, unless you have set StopAfterNoTrades to true, it will immediately place the 14 trades again and start over.

As MC says, you need to read everything and understand how the EA works.

Yep, that's the way this EA works. No need to be scared of the trim/reverses. You will surely see more than 2, but the EA will always come back into profit. In earlier versions that MetaCoder and I tested I have seen it recover from 25 or more trims and finally come back to take profit. The trick is to try to limit the number of trims required so that we take profit more quickly.

--- 帖子 #68 ---
Attached are 2 spreadsheets for your review and information. The one called Basket14_2010_01 is the same EA as Basket14_01 posted on this thread.

For information, so that you will know how to read these sheets, I keep statistics weekly, each week has a separate tab/sheet in the workbook. I sort the Account History by closing date/Time by clicking on the second column title "Time" towards the right side of the page. That shows you the sequence in which trades closed and gives a very clear picture of how the EA works. I then copy and paste the weekly info directly into my spreadsheet, color code the trim closings and have the spreadsheet calculate all the desired information.

When you open the attachment it will be on the latest week's report. You can click the tabs to the left along the bottom to view previous weeks reports.

You will note that Basket14_01 has been running since 25 July and has gained 10.4% profit. That is in spite of the fact that it went 2 straight weeks, 1 Aug - 13 Aug, without a close-all for profit.

Basket14_03 has only been running for 1 week and the last close-all netted almost 4% profit rather than the expected 1%. I have no explanation for that except possibly there was a strong move in favor of those trades at the time it was closing. Because of that anomaly it had a 6.5% gain for the week.

--- 帖子 #77 ---
I think what needs to be understood by more thread readers is that this strategy intentionally trims the biggest loser and opens an opposite-direction trade on the same pair whenever at least three losing pairs have breached their 24-hour high/low.

The way this is done is quite restrained, such that overtrimming is avoided. We want to do just enough trimming that we allow the same market action that triggered the trimming to take us to profit.

So do not be alarmed when the first actions taken by the EA make your balance shrink. If you are patient, a rise in equity will occur and all trades will be closed for profit.

There are old-school elements to this strategy, such as diversification (14 pairs), cut your losses early (cut the BIGGEST loser when market action makes it a logical decision), and let your winners run (until you come into profit).

--- 帖子 #91 ---
I'm running four different demos, each with a different leverage level. I have a 200:1, a 100:1, a 50:1 and a 10:1.

None of these has seen a margin level below 200% and all of them have gone through at least two profit-taking cycles ("legs" as they were called earlier).

You will notice that while one account's trades sit in positive profit, another's might be negative. This is because different pairs will be your biggest losers, and the cycles will sit at varying stages of maturity, depending on when you started the EA.

With patience, we always expect to see profit taken eventually, and sometimes much faster than we expect.

Another thing to notice is that this strategy does not care about pips, it does not track pips at all.

I see so many forum members talking in terms of pips, indicators, stop and limit levels, and usually within the context of trying to make steady profit from a single currency pair. A strategy like Basket14 will seem quite foreign to those who think that way.

--- 帖子 #123 ---
2.0 lots is not consistent with MaxMarginToUse set at 2.0 and a mini account that has $1,503.91. Sounds like the account is probably a standard account, not a mini.

Changing the default lot size from 0.1 to 0.01 will have no effect; that setting is an artifact from ancient EAs, sorry for the confusion.

The EA will work on a standard account, by the way.

Note that versions 02 and 03 put the burden on the user to make sure they're running the EA on an account with a big enough balance for the account type, whereas version 01 bails out if the balance isn't big enough for the account type.

I always recommend first running the EA on a demo account with the exact balance, leverage level and account type as the live account you want to run it on.  This will help avoid surprises and should be more than worth the extra effort.

If more people start trading these live, I'll do my best to identify the most common issues encountered and build safeguards and reminders into the EA.

--- 帖子 #135 ---
You have found the root cause of your problem. Probably those values are left over from running the EA on a previous account.

Close your chart which will stop the EA.

Hit F3 and and edit the global variables so that last flat balance and last flat equity are what they were before you started the EA, then close that window.

Repoen a chart and reattach the EA. Then you should see correct last flat balance/equity on your screen comments.

--- 帖子 #141 ---
Pluto2, note that in the short term, one account might look more favorable because of when the EA was started. A biggest loser on an EA that was started this morning will be a different biggest loser than on one that was started this evening, and the confirming losers will also be different.

In the long run, it comes out in the wash because when one account is waiting for the next equity pop, another is getting a good flow of cycles. Then they might switch places where the one that did the waiting is now the one getting the good equity pop frequency.

Version 03's use of the RVI indicator does nothing more than add a randomizing element to which direction to trade each side of the hedge. In your example, I'll bet 03 opened the trades in the opposite direction compared to 01. Is that true? If so, it was quite random.

On a somewhat related note, there are some mind-bending things I observed when I took time to track the two sides of this pure synthetic hedge. I wrote EAs that multiplied the exchange rates of each group of seven and then compared the two products after every tick. The two sides stay mostly equivalent at most given timepoints, though occasionally significant non-equivalencies did appear. IF one could have taken trades on the correct side at the EXACT exchange rates presented in certain time windows, one could SURELY have made profit.

The problem is that the non-equivalencies are corrected faster than the fourteen trades could be opened, thus destroying the advantage. I think in only one or two instances did I successfully detect and take advantage of significant non-equivalencies, take trades on them, and achieve profit. And from a heavily filtered, spread-manipulating broker like IBFX! It was cool to have my observations validated, but I saw that the trade frequency was not going to get anyone excited. If I could get TRUE transparency, paper-thin fixed spreads, and INSTANT (I mean a few milliseconds) execution, I guarantee I could use such a bot to make big profits in the safest imagineable way. However, the brokers understand that and have apparently put safeguards of some kind in place. Makes sense, I would too.

The mind-bending part is that, over time, the two sides' net movement over time can be such that one side's magnitude of movement is significantly more than the other's (mathematically equivalent to a GBPUSD long moving farther than a GBPUSD short when both were opened at the same time!!!). Yet somehow the single-timepoint equivalencies stay in place! Now a trader is left to wonder: will one side's greater motion continue in the same direction, and how much, and for how long, or will that motion immediately contract to compensate for the smaller movement on the other side? The answer is that these things are UNKNOWABLE and UNCONTROLLABLE. Add to that the fact that the broker can play with spreads at will, and you as the trader are left to figure out how as a coyote can you get a few morsels of sinew off the bones after the wolves are done.

Or, can you do better than that?

What kind of strategy can take advantage of directional movement when it occurs within a synthetic hedge basket, yet still maintain a mostly balanced set of positions?

In my mind, a strategy like Basket14 is one of the possible answers.

--- 帖子 #154 ---
Only because eTrader used that timeframe with the Looser strategy, that's the only reason.

As all signals are based on past information, it's mighty difficult to declare any signal "true" or "false".  Bigger timeframe indicators CAN uncover a longer-term and possibly more prevailing wind direction, but nothing is guaranteed when using past data to try to predict future events as I'm sure you know.

With version 03, I look at my usage of the RVI indicator as a randomizer -- nothing more, nothing less.

When I'm in a heavy development phase, I am always trying new things.

The "confirm" line of EAs is too specific in its confirmation criteria, I don't like it.

With the Basket14 series, I'm looking at different ways to improve entries so we come into profit sooner with greater frequency. I still haven't fully cracked the mysteries of the ebb and flow of how the two sides of the mathematically pure synthetic hedge move toward and away from each other (the question is not whether they do -- they most certainly do), and whether we can get a handle on it via composite RVIs or some other indicator.

I would love to find a way of identifying the outer limits of movement of the two sides of the hedge (version 05 is a stab, not quite in the dark, but not as precise as I'd like). I think I should try to enlist some indicator developers, some of whom appear to frequent this forum.

--- 帖子 #173 ---
We partially explored such a concept using "phantom trades".  This eliminates the need for a separate demo account.  We can take snapshots of exchange rates at a given time, pretend we have opened trades even though we did not, then track how our phantom trades would be doing, then open real trades (or not) based on what we see.

Your thinking is along a good line in my opinion, but I have limited time and energy to explore it with more EAs.

--- 帖子 #182 ---
Frazer, you might want to try Basket15_Add_01. You asked for something like this a while back, I believe.

Every hour it adds trades to winning pairs. The adder lot size is one tenth of the normal lot size, or the smallest lot size if one-tenth is below the smallest available lot.

A winning pair has to exhibit a profit at least as large as the dollar target in order to get a new trade added for it.

It's hot off the workbench, haven't tested it yet.

--- 帖子 #201 ---
I was wondering if the target cud be set in terms of fixed Dollars instead of % because what I see is lot of work for winner trades to meet the target once the equity reaches at certain level say $10,000 or $20,000. Any views.

--- 帖子 #202 ---
The target IS set in terms of fixed dollars. If you look at your screen comments you will see the dollar amount which is computed by taking 1%, or whatever you have set ProfitPct, of your LastFlatEquity (last close-all).

EDIT: If you feel 1% is too high you can always change it to a lesser %, say .05. This can be done at any time during the trading cycle. If you accumulate a lot of trims and get concerned about not getting to the Equity Profit Target soon enough, just open the Inputs window and change it - it will take effect immediately. That is not a recommendation, but if you are nervous that is a way to close out more quickly.

As your equity/balance grows, the EA will increase the lot size proportionately, which should offset the higher Dollar Profit Target.

--- 帖子 #213 ---
MC,

I am very impressed with your work and sharing.  Over time, I have read comments in forums about that "other similar strategy", and over and over again, the comment is always about severe drawdown.  You address this problem first and foremost - great job.

About initial selection of which group to Buy/Sell.  I have 5 thoughts on this.

1. Yes - it does matter about the selection and a random (or near random approach) will only extend CloseAlls.  Using a RSI on such a short time period on TF15 6 samples only gives you a short term view to what is going on.

2. Since the groups somewhat simulate the GBPJPY as per your analysis, Maybe we should look at Currency Strength for these two currencies. To Buy the first group, we would look for GBP to be in negative territory with a positive slope and JPY would be in positive territory and have a negative slope.  If we do not have this condition - go to thought 3.

3. Use a weighted approach evaluating each currency from their respective groups, and draw a decision based on weights.  If this does not draw a conclusive decision, go to thought 4.

4. Use a 21 prd H4 SAR instead of Currency Strength as in 2 and 3.   If this does not draw a conclusive decision, go to thought 5.  The SAR is  a great way to tune into the daily trend of a Pair.

5. Flip a coin.

Please take a look at the screen shot below for an idea of what I am talking about.

In closing, I have spent many months trying solve the DD problem using a variety of approaches and I never succeeded.  My input above is an attempt to help and to add a bit of edge to the strategy, but if it does not fit with your thinking - no problem.

KingHigh

--- 帖子 #217 ---
When you say drawdown are you referring to current balance compared to starting balance? If so, what you are seeing is normal for these EAs due to the strategy of trimming losers and reversing until the current EQUITY surpasses the LastFlatEquity. The hope is that the reversals will become winners, but in a choppy market that does not always happen, some will become winners and some will continue to be losers.

The balance will always go down with each trim. However, the reversed trades that do become winners plus the winning trades that continue to get more into profit will keep the equity high enough to make the account safe from margin calls and will eventually give you the 1% equity pop above LastFlatEquity. Sometimes that comes very quickly, sometimes it does not, but so far it has always happened eventually.

MC has repeatedly advised trading these EAs on demo accounts until you become comfortable with the "drawdowns" and confident in the ability of the EA to recover.

I, personally,have been working with MC on this concept and trading demos with each new version we develop for well over a year. The earlier versions had many names and we continued to improve the strategy with each new version. After all of that I am now confident that the Basket14 and Confirm14 EAs that MC has been kind enough to share on this forum will perform as expected. I have just started a live account with Basket14_01 this week (8 Sep) and I am very comfortable with it. I will sleep well this weekend even though that live account has not yet had an equity pop and has trimmed 5 times and all the reversed trades are currently losers and I still have a small negative PL. My drawdown by the above definition is a little over 5% but I'm confident that it will come into profit next week.

--- 帖子 #254 ---
I hear you Frazer and a version that does what you're saying would be easy to code now that I did the basic Add EA.

As I ponder it, I realize that I don't expect much difference between your suggestion and what currently exists.

Here's why.

If a loser is the Biggest Loser, it means it might have been the Biggest Winner if the trade had been in the opposite direction.

So in either case our new trade is one that is going in the "right" direction of a strongly moving pair.

But if we reverse a Biggest Loser rather than add a trade on an existing open pair, we maintain the balance of unique pairs in the basket.

This is my explanation for why I have hesitated to implement your suggestion.

Now if I think more positively about your suggestion, it's possible that UNdiversifying and allowing multiple trades on strong pairs could be a more winning way to go.

I guess we won't know unless I code it.

--- 帖子 #265 ---
This seems more like the trader101 approach where 7 buys and 7 sells are opened every Sunday. Let all buys settle down either on the top or bottom and sells on the opposite end. Trades taken in one direction when one of the buys from bottom crosses sell territory and reaches the top (safest approach); take all one way buys (14 trades) and vice versa when a sell reaches the top.

Try it out as I have been and it works fine. Lots of pips. Ofcourse there is a script to open and close all trades at once and there is one for locking profits.

This may be or may be not the right forum to mention this but just thought to due to similarity in approach.

--- 帖子 #286 ---
I'm interested!

--- 帖子 #287 ---
I think it's very good to mention it here!

Frazer is one of the people who told me about that strategy and we tried our own versions of it.

As many of you know, there is enormous market energy in these 14 pairs, and the fact that the two groups of seven form a perfect synthetic hedge makes it all the more interesting.

I remember scratching my head when Trader 101 said trading all 14 pairs in the same direction is the safest way to go, because clearly it's not.

It's safest to trade the two sets of seven in opposite directions, I think we would all agree.

One of the fascinating and compelling things is how much the two sides of the perfect hedge drift apart from each other.

If we can successfully quantify the extrema of the drifts, something very safe and successful should come about.  To measure drift, one has to establish an origin timepoint and measure motion from that point.  You get different results based on your origin timepoint, of course.

The best results would probably come from tracking motion against multiple origin timepoints.  I still haven't fully explored this but maybe others have looked at it more deeply.  Please share if you can!  Thanks!

--- 帖子 #296 ---
On the picture the colours don't show weary well but when the 2 lines for sell (red and yellow) comes from top and go under the middle line, and at the same time the 2 buy lines pass middle line and goes up its time to buy.

And when the opposite happen its time to sell.

The cross between the 4 lines show a trend shift between buy and sell of the 14 currency.

In the middle you also see a blue line and that line shows that the buy side is strongest. When the blue line is under the middle line, sell is the strong one.

--- 帖子 #321 ---
I just had an idea & so put a simple indicator together for it.  I'm not sure it's really of any use or how different it would actually work out being from using RVI to determine which way to open the baskets.

It calculates the linear regression of all pairs in each basket then gives each basket a score out of seven, which represents the number of pairs in the basket that are above their linear regression point.  The expectation is that they will revert to the linear regression point over time.

Therefore, if you had a score of say 6 for the first basket & 2 for the second basket you would sell the first basket & buy the second.  What do people think?

The defaults are 8 periods of 15min to calculate the numbers, but I don't know what would work best.

The code is not very pretty, feel free to use it, butcher it, or ignore it.

--- 帖子 #334 ---
In attempt to clear up questions the Oneway14_02 EA -- yes, clearly the EA can close for a loss.

What's causing it is closure when the RVI signal lines go above/below 0.0, which I thought would almost always provide profit when coming from a +/-0.15 level. I was wrong on that one!

As it turns out, SOMETIMES our entry criteria will get us to quick profit, but other times, it won't. Trading the whole basket of 14 in one direction is still NOT my favorite way to go and once again I've found more reinforcing evidence against doing it.

So now that both the entry and exit criteria haven't lived up to my expectations, I am tossing the underlying concept out the window. However, I will provide one more version that does not exit on RVI but still lets the trim'n'reverse do its thing.

On the other hand, the Add EA looks pretty good on my own demo and apparently on some of yours, too.

I'll pursue variations of Add, but more than that I still want to investigate some of the interesting in.dicators you guys have been offering in an effort to find a highly reliable way of picking the correct sides to buy and sell to get into fast profit via this pure synthetic hedge.

Thank you for all the testing and feedback. I'm sorry I can't implement all of the suggestions but I had to learn some time ago to carefully pick and choose which suggestions I explore. I haven't always picked correctly and at times I'll pick one that DOES NOT make sense to me just to prove to myself whether my judgment is sound or not. Sometimes good things have come from that kind of exercise.

Good trades to all.

Oneway14 version 03 does not exit on RVI but still lets the trim'n'reverse do its thing.

--- 帖子 #348 ---
Here is Basket14_03a. I'm not adding it to the first post since there is a 7-attachment limit per post.

I probably can't fully explain the entry criteria in plain English, but I'll try.

Let's start with the entry criteria for ver 03. That one only looks for the RVI of one group to be above the RVI of the other group to make its directional choice.

Ver 03a does that same thing, PLUS it looks for an exceedence of the midpoint between the highest RVI delta between the two groups and the average RVI delta over the last 100 15-minute bars before it enters.

So, 03a will sometimes be out of the market.

But it's exactly the same as ver 03 other than the entry logic.

And there is no guarantee it'll get us to profit any sooner. But it MIGHT and I thought this would be worth a try.

So here it is.

|

v

--- 帖子 #351 ---
MC,

Here is an example of what I am working on ( derived from work done by SMJONES - modified heavily) in an attempt to view the dynamics of the two groups.  I am working on displaying these charts as bars scaled to represent US Dollars.  The indies show:

1. Group1 pip bars     ( Red and Green Lines are Triple EMA of bar Bid )

2. Group2 pip bars     ( Red and Green Lines are Triple EMA of bar Bid )

3. Group1+2 pip bars  ( Red and Green Lines are Triple EMA of bar Bid )

4. Buy1/Sell2 net bars

5. Sell1/Buy2 net bars ( reciprocal of 4 )

Lines in 4 and 5 show Triple Ema of 1, 2, 3, 4, 5 day bars.

Darkest green is 1 day trend, Lightest green is 5 day trend.

I see some problems that I need to work on/debug/refine.  Nevertheless, maybe this sort of view can give us some insights on how to trade the Groups.

--- 帖子 #358 ---
Lots of ideas on the thread and I can't possibly code them all, but I usually code something so here is...something.

It's a ver 02 of the Add EA.  It uses one-tenth the customary lot size across the board and maintains that same small lot size for the added trades.  This is because sizes this small tip our accounts to profit on Add ver 01, so the initial trades shouldn't have to be large.  This should take our drawdown levels way down.

I thought about not opening the usual 14 at all but using the phantom trade technique instead, and then adding in trades as certain phantom pairs get to the defined profit levels.  This would have required dusting off old code that managed the phantoms and splicing it in with these newer EAs -- a bit more work.  Maybe I'll go that way eventually, don't know for sure yet.

In this version I am also using the new Basket14_03a entry logic to try to get a good edge on trade direction.

|

V

--- 帖子 #362 ---
Good, I thought we were on the same page.

Essentially it seems to me that what we are trying to do with these EA's is ride the contraction & expansion of the basket of currency pairs around the linear regression point (ie. mean reversion).  The indicator I knocked up was a very crude first attempt at trying to measure at which point we are in the cycle.  The big question is, over what time period should the regression point be calculated?  I chose two hours as a starting point because I noticed that when a basket closes in profit without any trimming that it generally is within a couple of hours.

Thinking more about this, what we really want to do is capitalise on those pairs which have deviated more from the reversion point than the others.  So how can we directly compare different pairs of different values?  How about measuring the standard deviations of the pairs from the regression point and then comparing them?  Perhaps with the "add" EA's the trigger to add trades could be once a pair has deviated noticeably compared to the other pairs?

I'm just spewing out ideas from inside my head, not saying any of it would actually work!

Also, I'm not exactly sure how the RVI calculates, maybe I am just going to end up basically recreating the RVI indicator with this?

--- 帖子 #363 ---
skoda, all I know from reading your posts is that you are trying to see, quantify and take advantage of the same thing I am -- expansion and contraction of the two sides of the hedge.

Here is an illustration of why I think we should include some kind of trim/reverse strategy to the add_01 EA. There are 2 $100+ losers and 5 of the 6 added trades are small losers. If those 2 big losers had been trimmed and reversed when they were -$45.30, Dollar Profit Target, the EA would have closed long ago.

I know that it will not always be this clear cut and the trim/reverse trades will sometimes not become winners, just as the added trades are not always winners. But it seems like we need something to counter what we are experiencing right now with this EA.

Here is another thought. Maybe we should just add a small trade in the opposite direction of any loser that exceeds minus the Dollar Profit Target, but I guess that gets us into a FIFO problem with US brokers.

--- 帖子 #388 ---
Just so everyone who may be using different leverage and MaxMarginToUse settings knows - MC did this by making MaxMarginToUse default to 0.1 rather than 1.0 as before. That setting is for a 100:1 leverage I think.

Those of us who were using other MaxMarginToUse settings with other than 100:1 leverage, need to set it to 1/10 of whatever we were using before. Before I realized this I had already started the EA with a setting of 0.2, as usual.

So forexripper, you and I need to reset MaxMarginToUse to 0.01, which won't make much difference in your $2000 account. It will just open .01 lots next time it opens the basket rather than the .02 it should have opened when you set it up as described above.

--- 帖子 #394 ---
Here is version 2 of what I have been working on.  It measures the linear regression point of each currency pair in the basket, then calculates the standard deviation away from the regression point and expresses it as a percentage of the current price.  What this means is the numbers of each pair can be directly compared.  A positive percentage means it's above it's regression point & you therefore want to sell it, negative means buy.

Over the weekend I will alter Basket14_01 to open the initial trades using this system.  I will experiment with two methods.  Firstly adding up the percentages for each basket & opening each basket in one direction, and secondly opening each individual currency pair in the direction calculated by the indicator.  Interestingly if you set the indicator to a slightly larger time frame often all of the currency pairs are in one direction - so maybe there is something to the open in one direction method?

--- 帖子 #397 ---
Tommy, you need to understand how the EA works and what the ET does. ET 3 will almost always be slower to take profit than ET 2 because the conditions to be met before trimming losers is more stringent. However, the trade off is that ET 2 will trim more often and cause larger drawdowns for hopefully short periods before taking profit. For folks who do not like to see several consecutive losing trades and big PL drawdowns in their account, ET 3 is the best way to go.

On a 100:1 acct using MaxMargin 2, I'm not sure what that looks like in number of lots per trade, but a trade at -200 may not be unusual at all. Before those biggest losers are trimmed, 3 pairs must have exceeded thier 24 hour High/Low. If you had a 3rd pair at -200 they might start closing, assuming 200 is the 24 hour high/low. On the other hand, Et 2 would have trimmed when the second pair hit -200.

Having said all that, there is a difference in brokers. GoMarkets is a non dealing desk broker so you get direct price feeds and they get processed much quicker and are not manipulated by the broker. I don't know anything about FxOpen, but if they use a dealing desk, that could account for some of the difference.

--- 帖子 #425 ---
As promised, here are some experimental files.

Firstly, an indicator which calculates the linear regression point of each pair, then calculates the standard deviation and represents it as a percentage of the regression point.  The only parameter to adjust is the regression period.  Default is 96 (15 minute periods) representing 24 hours.  It might be interesting to compare the values it generates against the existing EA's when they have trimmed a couple of times to see if the Buys & Sells are the same.

Secondly, I have modified Basket14_03 to buy or sell the baskets based on this indicator.  I have tried to keep the programming format the same, so as not to butcher Metacoder's code too much!  I have incorporated the indicator as a function at the end of the EA.

Thirdly, again Basket14_03 has been modified to buy or sell the individual currency pairs based on whether they have a positive or negative deviation from their regression point.

As Metacoder mentioned before (and I agree), it remains to be seen if using an indicator to buy/sell the baskets as a whole is anything more than a randomiser?  I think the individual buying/selling EA will be more interesting.

At the moment the EA's calculate their values based on ten 15 minute periods - just like Metacoder did with the RVI indicator.  I don't know if a longer time frame might be more appropriate?  It is a new input parameter that can be adjusted.

If this method turns out to be anything other than a failure, the percentage deviation could also be used as the trigger to trim & reverse or add trades.

It's the weekend, so these EA's are completely untested, I don't recommend using them for anything other than a bit of light hearted entertainment!

All EA´s put their 6 currency pairs long or short. Not 3 long and 3 short

--- 帖子 #430 ---
Here are my spreadsheets for this week on the 3 basket EAs I am running.

Basket14_01_ET2 has been running for 1 month and is up 18.33% compared to Basket14_01_ET3 which has been running for almost 2 months and is up 17.26%.

This week ET2 closed 7 times for 7.37% gain while ET3 closed 5 times for 5.14%.

I like ET 2 because it trims more quickly and takes profit more often. However, as I have said before, the trade off is that ET2 can occasionally trim numerous times between close-alls, which can cause some anxiety when trading live. Looking back through the weekly tabs you will find that ET3 has never had more than 4 consecutive trims and often reaches equity pop after only 1 trim, while ET2 has had as many as 6 and seldom reaches equity pop with only 1. My live account with ET2 started off with 11 trims before the first equity pop, and yes, I did feel some anxiety.

Basket14_Add_01 is very impressive after 1 week of testing. It closed out 5 times for 4.83% profit. Had I not started it with the defective initial EA, it would have performed even better. I am looking forward to next week testing 02, 04 and 02a

--- 帖子 #467 ---
Ignore the "Lot" variable when setting up the EA - it is known not to be used.

All that matters for lot sizing is the MaxMarginToUse (%) - It auto calcs the lot size for you.

I'd just like to highlight the fact that the max margin(lot size) calculated is not for all 14 trades - it is in fact for EACH trade.

So with 14 trades going at any one time (minimum - because of the possible further trim and reverse trades), like me, you may want to further reduce the MaxMarginToUse percentage so that the EA calculates for your trading style, a more comfortable lot size for each trade.

--- 帖子 #491 ---
Yes it is rolling 24 hours (meaning the last 24 hours from your last tick) - looking at the code, it will only trim when the ET has been met AND the biggest loser absolute value is greater than your current profit target AND that pair has exceeded the past 24 hour highest (if a sell)/lowest (if a buy)

e.g.

Biggest Loser = -$15, absolute value is $15, but Profit Target = $20, therefore no trim and reverse

Biggest Loser = -$20.01, absolute value is $20.01, but Profit Target = $20, will trim and reverse

--- 帖子 #518 ---
This is getting ridiculous having to explain dollar profit target and equity profit target over and over again. Some people just refuse to read or do not understand what they are reading.

E2u, you need to take the screen shot of the entire comment block. You have left out the only figure that really matters here, the current equity. The account PL makes no difference as far as when these EAs close. You are not in profit when you have a + PL. Your current equity must be more than the LastFlatEquity before you are in profit. When your Account Equity reaches the Equity Profit Target the EA will close and take the profit - has nothing to do with PL.

I sure hope we don't have to explain that again.

--- 帖子 #536 ---
Skoda2008,

I have been on the sidelines developing some tools to analyze the dynamics of the two baskets.  Frankly, I do not understand where we got the idea that Group 2 was a hedge for Group 1.  I believe that you noted the same thing in an earlier post. There seems to be a strong positive correlation between the two groups.

I also whole heartedly agree with your assessment that short term trend is of little value in determining basket direction.  What is more important is the longer term trend such as daily/weekly - or the old standby - the 200 SMA.

I have an indicator that displays basket candles in US Dlrs for all configurations of buy/sell of the two groups with net results - all pips wins and losses are displayed in dollars - candles and histograms.

I am currently in a stop and think mode about where to go next with my work. I have currency strength indicators that could possibly be a help.

BTW - I have a n-order polynomial curve fit indicator that is a super set of the linear regression calculation that you use that could be of interest to you.

KingHigh

--- 帖子 #558 ---
MaxMarginToUse is the percent of your account value that will be used to open new trades. If we double MaxMargin it doubles the lot size we are trading. Therefore we should expect to double the profit by cutting in half the time it takes to reach the Profit Target. But I don't think that is the case with these EAs because both the winners and losers are double, so it takes just as long to reach the Profit Target.

--- 帖子 #572 ---
I haven't had a chance to test this yet. With this much code, bugs are almost inevitable because even when I think I nailed it on the first try, there is usually at least one issue.

This will not open real trades until at least one phantom trade is 20 pips in the good. If that is the case during minute 0, trades will be added in the direction of pairs that have gained at least 20 pips. You can change the default 20 by altering the PipTarget4Add setting.

You can track phantom buy and phantom sell pips in the screen comments. I list pips by individual pair, by phantom buys as a group, by phantom sells as a group, and then as an entire group.

It is complicated to track phantom PL by dollar amount and I can surely crack that little problem given time, but for now I have chosen pips. Yes I do know what's involved code-wise, so no need to chime in, you coding wizards out there.

Default for MaxMarginToUse is 0.2, default for ProfitPct is 1.0. I intend to test with these settings on a 50:1 leveraged demo.

There is significant new code here (actually some older code surgically fitted into the newer Add code), so don't expect bug-free operation at first.

Please report anomalies you see and I'll upload corrections as soon as I can. I'm busier than usual these next several days all the way through the weekend so please be patient.

|

V

--- 帖子 #575 ---
Frazer, if this sounds familiar, it should, because it's VERY close to a phantom-based EA we did a while back.

There are some key differences, though.

One, we only let 14 trades get opened with the old EA. Two, we used much more margin per trade. Three, we trimmed losers at a regular interval.

With this new EA, we are not imposing a limit on the number of trades we can open, despite the presence of the MaxTrades setting. It's not used, I didn't mean to leave it in [UPDATE: just removed it and reuploaded].

We are using much less margin per trade.

We are not trimming losers.

My intent is for this to behave a lot like Add_01 but without the original basket of 14 opened as real trades.

--- 帖子 #586 ---
This is Basket14_Add_01 without the initial basket of trades, which are being performed by the phantoms. The add trades are traded in whatever direction the phantom winner is trading, just as the add-on trades in Bskt_Add_01 were. There should be no need for a trim and reverse strategy, just as there was none in Bskt_Add_01. And there are no "safety stops" in any of these EAs.

That will most assuredly happen - all the trades will not be winners, but the assumption here is that most of them will be, as they have been in Bskt_Add_01. The MaxMarginToUse is 0.2 and you can make it less if it makes you feel any better. On my $5000 standard 100:1 leveraged demo it opens .01 lot for each trade, so we're not talking about a lot of margin being used per trade. It would take a whole bunch of losing trades to put the account in jeopardy.

I know I should probably not be answering your questions since I'm not a programmer and you are, but it seemed to me that you did not understand what we are trying to do with this EA. I'm sure MC will give you a better explanation.

--- 帖子 #595 ---
I saw your results and understand why the Phantom EA was created, but looking at one of your earlier trading rounds, I saw this:

+63.86  Original Trades PL

-20.95  Added Trades PL

I looked further to understand why...

It was mainly because GBPUSD was greater than the DollarProfitTarget most hours of that round, so the EA kept adding trades to it.

BUT!  What the EA failed to track was the initial trade's hourly progress.

If it did track the hourly progress, then it wouldn't have added more trades when it noticed that the pair was slowly pulling back in terms of the initial trade's last hour's profit.

e.g.

Hour1: GBPUSD initial trade is now +60 and greater than DollarProfitTarget... Woohoo! Let's add a 10% lot!

Hour2: Now +61 and still >DPT... ooh the added trade is now +1, lets add another 10% trade

Hour3: Now +58 but still >DPT... oh noes... the added trades are now -5 in profit combined... hmmm, let's not add any more trades this hour

etc...

etc...

--- 帖子 #603 ---
I believe the essence of what you're saying is that all trades on a pair should be positive before adding more trades to the pair. That AUTOMATICALLY means hourly progress has been positive, or at least the spirit of your idea is supported.

Maybe there are several trades open on a pair, and an hour comes where a couple of them pulled back. At minute 0 of that hour, no trades would be opened on it. But if one hour later all trades on the pair were positive, we have forward progress and we'd open another trade on the pair.

Of course, if no trade has been opened for a pair yet, we would allow a new trade on it.

|

v

Hi MetaCoder,

I found a bug in the Phantom EAs

This line in AddIfNeeded():

Inserted Code for (i = GBPUSDidx; i < EURCHFidx; i++)

Needs to be:

Inserted Code for (i = GBPUSDidx; i <= EURCHFidx; i++)

because the EURCHF symbol won't get traded on.

--- 帖子 #650 ---
^ No, because it would behave exactly the same.

The purpose of this indicator is to have a graphical representation of the GROUP deviations from their (implied) mean.  I intend to use it to run along side the original basket_01 and see if the fastest successful closures correspond to a difference between the deviations above a certain threshold.  That threshold is yet to be determined.  If there is some kind of connection then it could be used as the basis to buy or sell each group,  and possibly determine when to sit aside.  This would work whether they are real opening trades or phantom ones.

Because it now shows historical deviations it is possible for anyone who has being keeping trade records of the current EAs to compare them against this indicator and see if there is a pattern.

--- 帖子 #671 ---
Skoda2008,

Looked at your MultiPair indy and would like to make an observation.

When doing any sort of cross currency pair calculations, you can never assume that the bar of one pair has a matching bar in the other currencies at the same time.  Unless -- you have perfect history data, which I have never had. Once there is a missing bar in any currency, the problem just accumulates.

On an EA that I was developing for a hedge between EURUSD and USDCHF, I HAD the holygrail until I figured out that the bars were missaligned and I was using future data from USDCHF for caluclations.  Oh Well - big disappointment.

SoOOO - I use the following for each pair:

baseTime = iTime("EURUSD",0,bar); // probably the most complete set of bars

targetBar = iBarShift(TargetPair,0,baseTime,FALSE);

or more concise:

targetBar = iBarShift(TargetPair,0,iTime("EURUSD",0,bar),FALSE);

Hope this helps.

KingHigh

--- 帖子 #674 ---
I know this is a bit off topic, but it is important.

I hope all you developers take note of what KingHigh mentioned. From what I have seen, this is a very common mistake made by amateur (and professional) MT4 coders. In fact, many of the so-called "best" programmers on FF make this error. As KingHigh has witnessed, it can certainly lead to invalid data and invalid backtest (visual and otherwise) results.

Obviously, this error has more chance of causing invalid data on the lower timeframes (M1, M5) where gaps in history are more likely. Nevertheless, it is a good habit to never, ever assume the shift for one symbol will be the same for a different symbol.

Bravo KingHigh!!

You need to be very careful about what MaxMargin you use for what leverage level. As MC pointed out it is not advisable to trade a very small standard account. --- 帖子 #732 ---
I don't think everyone understands that a 0.01 lot size on a mini account is different from a 0.01 lot size on a standard account, though I'm sure most understand it fully.

And how many folks completely understand the exact nuances of managing multiple pairs in the context of point, tick size, tick value, symbol name mangling, etc?

Then you throw in the slightly complex settings of the EAs, and it's hard to keep things uniform for all users.

Another obstacle -- human impatience.  Traders see an EA get good results fast, because sometimes that can happen, then expect that kind of result on any given day, regardless of what kind of market action we're having.

However, I still strive to get it all correct and robust so anyone can throw these EAs on just about any broker's MT4 demo and get good results.

I hope people will understand if I don't respond to every query about why I made a certain code change, or why isn't this EA giving me great results today.

Good trades to you all.

well it is indeed a confusing topic, because in the typical description we are all used to:

standard account used to mean you could only trade 1.0 lot size minimum, meaning $10/pip on EU

mini account used to mean you could trade .10 lot size minimum, meaning $1/pip on eu

micro account used to mean you could trade .01 lot size minimum, meaning 10cents/pip on EU

How you and MC are defining them I am not sure, but that was always my understanding.

--- 帖子 #744 ---
The big thing to look at is how much does PL change in dollar terms for each tick for a trade of x lots that you have open. Then you can look at the math behind lot sizes, tick values, tick sizes, points, margin, leverage...

There are indeed several confusing terms used by traders and brökers and EA programmers, and they don't always mean the same thing. You have to come up with your own understand to get to the bottom of it.

Here is one example of confusion: TICK VALUE. Does tick value mean the dollar-cent value on one tick, or one pip -- but hey wait a minute aren't ticks and pips the same? -- or one fractional pip, or on the last three pips that were covered by the previous market tick, or on the last three ticks that were covered by the previous market fractional pip, or...

Or how about this: when you say "nanolot" or "microlot", do you mean it in the context of a micro account, or a mini account, or a standard account, and how exactly do you define a micro, mini or standard account?

See how this can get confusing?

--- 帖子 #776 ---
Thank you MetaCoder, frazerd and all contributers of this great thread!

I just finished reading all posts, FAQ and source code (partially).

Allow me two system (Basket14) relevant questions:

1) After reviewing the source code, I wonder why after profit taking (Equity Pop) all basket pairs are reopened in their default trade direction. It would be obvious for me to trade each reopened pair in the direction of its last profit (if BUY/SELL was in profit then buy/sell else sell/buy). So we have better chances to follow the immediate trend and probably avoid unnecessary cut-reverse.

2) Margin and traders nerves don't like too much drawdown. On non US brokers hedging of single basket pairs in loss could solve the problem. E.g. we open a (1:1) hedge trade for every pair more than say 100 pips in loss. If the pair gets cut then our hedge trade becomes the new basket trade and if the pair comes back (no cut), we can close it's hedge at break even. What we reach is less drawdown and less pressure on margin and nerves.

ps: I will start demo testing as soon I have setup a private server.

--- 帖子 #791 ---
Sir, there are reasons why the EAs here will not take the directions you mention.

Your first suggestion assumes that there might be further momentum in one direction, and I'm saying there is no assurance of that and that it's just as reasonable to assume there will be movement in the opposite direction.

I will not code any same-pair hedges within these systems.  I should point out to you that even if I did, the same-pair-hedged trades will NOT close at breakeven since you specified waiting until we are at 100 pip losses before opening the hedges.  So at best we will have 100 pips losses per same-pair-hedged pair, will we not?  I say this as someone who has extensive experience designing and implementing same-pair hedge strategies.

I don't reject your suggestions lightly and I don't want to blast your first post on the forum.  I know you made your comments in good faith but I ask you to entertain the possibility that I thought of those things a good long while ago, and have good reasons why I don't pursue them.

I'll close by saying I provide full source code to every EA so that if you believe strongly in an idea, you have every opportunity to implement the idea yourself.

--- 帖子 #797 ---
Here is a surprise. This is the one that trims and reverses losers as well as adding to winners. I started it on 9/16 and it accumulated a large number of add-on trades without a close-all. So I had pretty much forgotten about it and was not watching it closely. On 9/28 it closed 582 trades, having previously trimmed and reversed 10 times. It took about 13 minutes to close them all and by the time it finished it had almost 2% profit rather than 1%.

On 9/28 through this morning it closed 4 more times for an additional 4.42% profit.

I had the Exceedence Trigger set to 2, thus the large number of trims and unacceptable -2302 Largest Floating Loss, -32% Max Floating Drawdown and 226.5% Lowest Margin on a 500:1 account. Had I left the ET at 3, it would have trimmed much less, may have closed sooner and those unacceptable stats would probably not have occurred. I have changed ET back to 3 today.

Another improvement to this one would be the Add_01a strategy of not adding trades on a pair that does not have all winning add-ons.

This once again shows the resilience and ability of these EAs to come back into profit after a seemingly unrecoverable drawdown.

pairs that are -20 pip or greater in loss, get a real trade opened that is the reverse direction of the phantom trade.

--- 帖子 #821 ---
Fredgold, I have trouble remembering what the difference is in these also, so I will try to explain it to you and refresh my own knowledge at the same time.

Phantom_Add_01 was the original. It uses phantom trades on the 14 pair basket and those are expressed in pips. Every hour it opens a real trade of any phantom that is +20 pips or more. No real basket trades are ever opened.

Phantom_Add_02 is the same as 01 except that it will not open a trade on a pair that has previous trades that are negative. The intent is to not keep making trades on a pair that has reversed, but is still above the +20 pips.

Phantom_Add_01a is the same as 01, but the phantoms are expressed in dollars and real trades are opened on any pair that exceeds 1/10 of Dollar Profit Target.

Phantom _Add_01a_the-game is a combination of 01a and 02. The phantoms are expressed in dollars, every hour a real trade is opened on any pair that exceeds 1/10 of Dollar Profit Target, but only if all previous trades on that pair are winners.

Also, in all the Phantom EAs where there are no trim and reverses, the floating PL does show the actual drawdown of the account - equity will always be the balance + PL. That should make some of you happy.

I hope this helps - it helped me anyway.

--- 帖子 #830 ---
Taz,

Please correct me if I am wrong and I apologize if I am. You have in your code:

if (TimeMinute(TimeCurrent()) != 0 || TimeMinute(TimeCurrent()) != 30) ClearSymbolMarks();

Shouldn't this be

if (TimeMinute(TimeCurrent()) != 0 && TimeMinute(TimeCurrent()) != 30) ClearSymbolMarks();

If you have an OR condition, it will always be true regardless of the Minute.

If the minute = 0 - the 2nd part will be true (Minute != 30).

If the minute = 30, the 1st part will be true (Minute != 0).

If the minute is something other than 0 or 30, say 15. both parts will be true.

The statement will be True all of the time, for every minute.

If you change the OR to and AND condition, it won't be true on Minutes 0 and 30.

If you do see this happening after the fix, just reduce the ProfitPct from 1.0 to 0.5 to get faster equity pops.

Beware - MaxMarginToUse is totally different in the phantom EAs. The 1.0 for 200:1 leverage was for opening the basket trades, not add-ons. EDIT: Add-ons in the Bskt_Add EAs were 1/10 the size of the basket trades. When MC wrote the Phantom EAs he increased the size of the added trades, but still kept them small enough to not endanger your account. I would not use 1.0 - at that lot size your account will be very vulnerable if you get several trades open and they are not winners.

--- 帖子 #858 ---
Fred, you need to look at your Dollar Profit Target, then use a multiple that will put your highest phantoms at or near or maybe above the target. It is your call. MC has provided the basics, now it's up to us to make it work for our trading preferences. Most of us don't trade with as high a balance as you, so we don't have the problem. Since your profit target is 1000(+), if you wanted a phantom with +$10 value to be close to the trigger, you would need to use 100 as the multiple, making it $1000. If you want +$5 to reach the target use 200. The multiple multiplies all your phantoms by that amount and then checks to see if any have reached the target.

--- 帖子 #872 ---
I've been testing a concept for a while and will test it for a while longer before I post EAs that implement it.

The concept is to open trades during minute 0 when a pair is the biggest phantom winner (in dollars/cents, not pips).

This tends to limit the number of trades and I have verified that it can get us to profit. It also avoids having to mess with proportionality; we bypass the need for comparing a phantom trade's PL against DollarProfitTarget.

This concept can be applied to all 14 pairs or to a subset of the pairs, such as the ones found in AddSix.

I've verified that equity pop can be reached this way.

A further restriction you can add is to only add a trade when all other trades on that pair are in profit, as we have done elsewhere. I don't know how many of us are fond of that criterion.

--- 帖子 #873 ---
I intend to refine the Phantom idea as much as possible.  I like it the best of anything.

--- 帖子 #874 ---
The first AddSix EA, and the only one posted here so far, adds trades on any phantom pair that is in profit during minute 0.  That criterion is very loose so it can lead to a lot of trades.  My demo finally closed a LOT of trades for profit on Friday.  Margin had gotten dangerously low.

I then started running an AddSix version that only opens a trade for a pair if it is the biggest phantom winner in minute 0.  This gave me a much quicker profit closure.

This is one of my observations that validates the tactic of trading biggest phantom winners.

--- 帖子 #883 ---
No, you will not need to reset global variables, just change the multiplier.

Yes, StopAfterNoTrades does work. If it is true the EA will not trade again after the next close-all until you change it back to false. You would use that to stop the trading while you change the multiplier. Then when the multiplier is the way you want it change StopAfterNoTrades back to false and it will start trading again when your phantoms reach the target.

--- 帖子 #903 ---
My current stream of consciousness about the forex market...

When we view currency pairs as numerator/denominator entities where a single currency is either a numerator or a denominator (that's all they are, correct?), the two 7-pair sides of our 14-pair hedge are mathematically equivalent. So if we multiply the exchange rates of both sides at any point in time, we should get the same numerical result.

I've run EAs that do these multiplications and comparisons in real time, monitoring for distortions. Remarkably, the two sides of the hedge stay equivalent within a range that doesn't allow for profitable exploitation (we have to overcome spread, remember), save for very occasional distortions that are quickly corrected.

However, if you map the movement of the two sides of the hedge, they DO drift apart over time, then drift back together. There is no telling which side of the hedge will move more than the other, we can only observe it when it does happen. We observe it when we open trades where one side is bought and the other is sold, and our account sees a floating loss or a quick profit, neither of which should happen. But it happens because of the sides moving to different extents.

WAIT A MINUTE, you say to yourself. What is going on?

If at single-timepoint snapshots the two sides of the hedge stay roughly equivalent almost always, yet they move apart and back together over time, wouldn't that mean at least one currency pair among the 14 pairs might appear to be used as a "pressure relief valve" or something like that?

Let's step back for a moment and try looking at it from the banks' and the brökers' points of view. They know that smart traders out there are looking at these synthetic hedges and are trying to profit from momentary distorations that should not exist. They can't give away free money just for being smart enough to do a little multiplying and comparing!

Some mechanism has to be in place to keep the distortions under control. One thing that can be done is to play with spreads. If a distortion gets large enough that a sophisticated trader could profit from it, the spreads can be increased to defeat the trader's advantage.

Another thing that can be done to keep the distortions in check is to continually adjust exchange rates of selected pairs, a little at a time, to keep things in equilibrium despite the movement that's happening.

My belief at this time is that EURCHF, EURGBP and GBPCHF are among the pairs that are adjusted to keep the distortions in check as the individual pairs move due to trading action. This is why they pop up as biggest phantom winners as often as they do.

Thoughts?

--- 帖子 #904 ---
Open every half hour if trades are the biggest phantom winners or the biggest phantom losers (traditional direction reversed if losers). Require that all preexisting trades on the pair be in profit.

--- 帖子 #914 ---
First post, I know...  I have been following the thread for a while and am a fan of the ideas here and MetaCoder's coding.  Thought I would chime in with my update to the code in case it helps future iterations:

1. Added an extern variable for add interval.  This is in minutes and a MathMod is done to determine if we should check for adding positions:

...

if (MathMod(TimeMinute(TimeCurrent()), AddMinuteInterval) == 0) ClearSymbolMarks();

if ((BidsHaveChanged &&

(MathMod(TimeMinute(TimeCurrent()), AddMinuteInterval) == 0) &&

!CloseAll))

...

- Example Values: 60 = every hour; 30 = every 30 minutes; 15 = every 15 minutes, etc. (don't set it to 0...)

2. Added an extern variable called OnlyAddAllInProfit.  Possible values TRUE or FALSE.  If true, then all trades have to be in profit for additions.  If false, don't add on:

...

if (SymbolArray[i] == BiggestPhantomWinnerSymbol &&

(!OnlyAddAllInProfit || (OnlyAddAllInProfit && AllSymbolTradesInProfit(SymbolArray[i]))) &&

!SymbolMarked(SymbolArray[i]))

...

Hope I'm not stepping on anyone's feet and I hate to add another version to the mix, but it seemed that some people like the every hour addition, some people like the all-in-profit option, and some don't.

Version 01a: Same as 01, but also reset the phantom trades during minute 0 of every hour. This should let us detect direction changes much sooner.

--- 帖子 #929 ---
You guys probably have the feel now for how each new blend of tactics is not based on perfect trading wisdom, just a few tools in the bag that have been proven to work quite often, added to new ideas as they arise. Of course we filter any proposed blend of known proven tactics and new unproven tactics through what we THINK is a decent understanding of forex mechanics, but we always assume we must see our ideas in action for a while before we declare them good.

Our process for improvement is based on, "Hey, here's something to try, let's code it up and give it a whirl, then analyze why it works or doesn't work and repeat the process until a better strategy emerges."

We got where we are through this process, and we're keeping that process intact.

Obviously, the goal is to get more frequent profit and fewer situations where we get big drawdown. Waiting for things to happen when the market is quiet or strange isn't a problem. But those other two things, we want and continue to pursue them doggedly.

--- 帖子 #942 ---
Have a look at your ORIGINAL mod from Add_02.taz and have a look at mine (that I recently posted a few posts back) at that same line.

They look different, but in fact they produce the same result.

As dim13 pointed out your mod would always be true, therefore ClearSymbolMarks() would always be called.

That is why I commented out that if statement.

NOTE: ClearSymbolMarks() just clears all pairs that they have already been marked as added.

In reality your mod does not need to call ClearSymbolMarks() at all as long as the !SymbolMarked(SymbolArray[i]) && MarkSymbolAdded(SymbolArray[i]) code is removed.

--- 帖子 #943 ---
Now for the *fixed* taz-mod you just have to add this line in front of the ClearSymbolMarks() code:

Inserted Code if (TimeMinute(TimeCurrent()) != 0 && TimeMinute(TimeCurrent()) != 30)

But as I said last week, this mod will not allow the EA "ride" the momentum, so you would need a smaller ProfitPct value.

*** EDIT: This means that it will only be able to add once every half hour.

--- 帖子 #979 ---
Simple example:

Buy EURUSD and Sell EURUSD, that's a same-pair hedge.

For a synthetic hedge, you could

Buy EURUSD, Sell EURJPY, Buy USDJPY; this is a synthetic hedge because you have

Bought EUR

Sold USD

Sold EUR

Bought JPY

Bought USD

Sold JPY

See how everything is balanced?

Within the AddSix EA, we have two synthetic hedges, and these synthetic hedges exist as a subset within our big 14-pair synthetic hedge of:

Group 1, The Phantom Buys

1. GBPUSD

2. EURGBP

3. GBPJPY

4. USDCHF

5. NZDUSD

6. AUDJPY

7. EURJPY

Group 2, The Phantom Sells

8. EURUSD

9. USDJPY

10. AUDUSD

11. NZDJPY

12. GBPCHF

13. CHFJPY

14. EURCHF

The following illustration tries to shed light on WHY it's a synthetic hedge.  Currency pairs are properly viewed as numerators and denominators.  So in the picture we show GBPUSD as GBP above USD.  Note how certain numerators and denominators cancel out.  After the canceling, the same currencies exists in the numerators and the denominators for both sets of 7.

http://members.cox.net/rcochran/supercurrencies.jpg

--- 帖子 #1001 ---
Only that the pairs traded are limited to EURCHF, GBPCHF and EURGBP.

You could take AddSix 02 and modify the logic to only trade EURCHF, GBPCHF and EURGBP and you'd have the Add_04.

The good results are partly due to using a bröker with tiny spreads. The downside with that bröker is that you have to pay a monthly fee. I tried the same EA with IBFX and it didn't open enough trades to be worthwhile. Big spreads on those pairs get in the way.

A good thing to keep in mind is that the policymakers, bankers and brökers over the last few years have added little annoying things to make it hard to do well as retail traders. Swap/interest rates were adjusted to keep us from accumulating swap money on certain pair combinations, same-pair hedging was eliminated unless you follow FIFO (or however it is now), ticks are heavily filtered to keep us from exploiting distortions, leverage has been decreased (probably good for the many clueless traders who haven't bothered to self-educate about margin, leverage, etc.), brökers adertise "low spreads" but freely increase them when it serves their purposes, brökers flag and disallow various trading styles and trade against our positions... and that's just a partial list.

--- 帖子 #1009 ---
My new mod idea (which might have been what thegame was playing with not sure) is working nicely so far.  Most legs are opened and close within 15 mins, was pretty fun to watch last night.

However, I do think a weakness to this one, as well as the add_02.taz mod, is the timing of the new legs.  From what I see so far in testing, I am of the opinion that a cycle that is opened toward the end of the us session is typically the one that creates the dd.  Obviously things slow down quite a bit, asian retracements occur, etc.  So what ends up happening alot of times, about 1900 or after, a cycle starts up.  Then just flounders around until a bit before london open, but is adding trades all during that time.  Then at london open, we have to just pray like hell that it doesnt take off in the wrong direction of our basket, when momentum and volume takes off.

So, what I propose, and maybe someone can help me with this.

At 0500GMT, the ea can turn on and start taking basket trades.

At 1900GMT, the ea continues what it is doing if it is in a basket cycle already, continuing to add to trades as it's coded to etc.  However, the stopafternotrade flag is set to true, without affecting or refreshing the ea.  Once the basket leg is closed in profit, the ea sleeps and takes no more baskets, until 0500GMT, when it awakens and does it all over again.

If someone would be kind enough to help me out in adding this code, I am more than happy to share the latest mod I am working with.

P.S. Yes, this can easily be done manually, just change the flag to true at 1900GMT, however this action resets the ea, so all phantom calculations are reset to 0 and it affects the current basket cycle continuing to do what it needs to do.

Here's my chart for the 18 hours of testing i've done so far.  The 6% dd happened during the time I am trying to avoid with the above, and the second dip happened because my damn pc crashed due to another crazy ea I am playing with while I was sleeping last night.  Regardless, 10% gain in 18 hrs isn't too bad   And most baskets are closed before I even notice they were opened lol

--- 帖子 #1022 ---
The name is appropriate - the EA STOPS after no trades - when it has closed for equity pop profit. The intent was to give you a chance to withdraw or add funds to your account while the EA was stopped and then start it again when the money transactions were complete. Otherwise the margin to use and lot sizes would get screwed up when adding orwithdrawing money.

Reference the code required to only trade during specific hours, MC has that coded in a Looser EA we were working with before starting this thread. He may be willing to post the code for you to use. Or you can extract it from the EA yourself. It's LooserKissMe_08 located at http://www.forexfactory.com/showthre...36#post3976836

--- 帖子 #1029 ---
Initially, buy the phantom-buy group of pairs and sell the phantom-sell group of pairs.

Every hour, add a trade to the phantom pair that is the biggest phantom winner. Also add a reverse trade to the phantom pair that is the biggest phantom loser. Before adding any trades, require that no trades exist on the pair, or that all preexisting trades on the biggest phantom winner/loser pairs be in profit. There is no symbol marking in this version as it is redundant with the check for preexisting trades being in profit.

Close reverse/"wrong-way" trades if they hit one-tenth of DollarProfitTarget. This is the "gravy" profit.

Let me know if it doesn't appear to be trading as intended, there's a brand new function called TakeWrongwayProfit.

|

v

--- 帖子 #1054 ---
Some versions here use reverse technique in form of: PipTarget4Reverse and BiggestPhantomLoserSymbol (inside function: AddIfNeeded), which is a clever implementation.

But only 1 trade of a pair in the wrong direction blocks a possible profitable reversal => AllSymbolTradesInProfit(SymbolArray[i])

E.g., today we had a strong intraday reversal in GBPCHF. A change from BiggestWinner to BiggestLooser, but I saw that handling this was impossible because of AllSymbolTradesInProfit(SymbolArray[i]) and the loss in GBPCHF (morning buy) grow bigger and bigger.

Wouldn't it be necessary to stop these big loosers, after they switched to the opposite side of the virtual hedge (or perhaps earlier)?

--- 帖子 #1065 ---
Just for clarification, MC, are you using a IBFX mini account with 50:1 leverage and writing the EAs for that set up? I think that is the case and many brokers do not even offer a "mini" account as defined by IBFX where 1 pip equals 1 cent. So, those who do not have the mini account capability should be reducing the MaxMarginToUse setting accordingly on all these EAs. Just because a broker offers 2 decimal place pricing, that does not equate to a mini account. And, as MC said, $2000 is a pretty small account if you are not on a IBFX type mini account.

--- 帖子 #1080 ---
Fred, the magic number is used by the EA to keep track of the trades, etc, belonging to that EA. There is no need to ever change a magic number unless you are using 2 or more EAs on the same account. In that case each EA must have a unique magic number so that each EA can control it's own trades.

Vienna is running 2 EAs on the same account and thus needs 2 different magic numbers.

--- 帖子 #1142 ---
Vienna, your screen comments tell the story. Your Last Flat Equity was 2033.15. That could have been left from a previous EA running on the same account. If so, you can change it from the Extras tab at the top of the page - Extras > Global Variables or F3 key. Change the Last Flat Equity to your current Equity.

The Dollar Profit Target is 20.33 and that gives you a Equity Profit Target of 2053.48. The EA will close when your Equity exceeds 2053.48 unless you change the Last Flat Equity.

You are also showing a Lowest Margin % of 48.66%, which could also be left from a previous EA with the same Magic Number. You can also change that using the F3 key to reflect your current Margin Level.

The problem is that all our EAs have the same Magic Number, so when you put a new EA on a platform that had previously been running another of these EAs, it will pick up the Global Variables that are pre-existing on the platform.

--- 帖子 #1160 ---
Here is another screenshot of Phantom_AddSix_02. It now has 11 trades, all GBPCHF and all losers. You may remember from the screenshot I posted this morning that GBPCHF was the biggest winner at +$2.17. At 2300 it was still the biggest winner. It is now at $1.71 and it looks like EURGBP has moved up to take over as biggest winner, but EURGBP is not one of the 6 pairs we are adding so GBPCHF will continue to be my only pair. Seems to me that puts my account well outside the framework of the balanced hedge and if the GBPCHF continues it's upward move and accelerates, I will have 11 trades that will become big losers rather than small ones and it will send my equity way down.

I guess my point is that none of these EAs stays within the framework of a balanced hedge. The profit comes from being out of balance in the right direction. But we have yet to come up with a system that ensures we are always on the right side of a big move, so regardless of which EA we are using there is always that chance of getting into a low equity situation. As you can see from my screenshot, AddSix_02 is certainly not low-equity-proof.

Just my thoughts on the matter for what they're worth.

--- 帖子 #1170 ---
The hedge is not always in place in terms of open trades. But if the wind shifts before profit is reached, the other side of the hedge will be exploited to open new trades.  So I'll stick to my position that the EAs' underlying strategies (except for the "wrongway/taz" tactic) are within the framework of a balanced hedge.  A glance at the open trades often doesn't reveal the hedge.

--- 帖子 #1196 ---
The Maxmargin settings need to be appropriate for the leverage. With this EA (phantom_Add_02-taz) 0.1 seems to be perfect for 500:1 leverage. The smaller the leverage the larger MaxMargin can be and remain safe. Although I used the term aggressive settings, that doesn't mean you should increase the MaxMargin. I think some people reporting on this thread may be using the default 0.4 on 500:1 and 400:1 accounts. That is aggressive and is probably the reason for their poor performance reports.

I cannot tell you how to set your account, because I have not tested other settings. However, it would seem reasonable to assume that if 0.1 is good for 500:1, then 0.2 may work for 400:1, 0.3 for 300:1, 0.4 for 200:1, etc. The only way to know for sure is to test it and see what happens.

I am using the default 0.4 on my 50:1 account and that is working, but not as well as the 500:1 account. After this week I will probably try increasing it to 0.5 and then to 0.6. However, there is a point of no return at the lower leverage levels. You have to keep watching the lowest margin and make sure it does not get to an unacceptable level. I believe MC has stated that 200 - 300% is acceptable for 100:1 and 50:1 leverage. And, of course, the size of the account will also influence the lowest margin level. The more money you have, the less the MaxMargin setting will affect lowest margin.

--- 帖子 #1198 ---
Taz is correct. That EA checks once every hour to see what phantom trade is the biggest winner. If the biggest winner is one of the 6 pairs (EURCHF, EURJPY, CHFJPY, GBPCHF, GBPUSD, USDCHF) it places a real trader for that pair. It continues to do that until the Equity is ProfitPct (1.0 default) above Last Flat Equity. Then it closes all trades for the specified profit and starts over again.

These EAs never close just losers. They always wait until the sum of losers and winners is positive and always close for profit, never for loss. Having said that I must also warn that in a fast moving market, if there are a large number of trades to close, it can result in a loss, even though there was a profit when the EA started closing.

--- 帖子 #1206 ---
You are using 400:1 leverage, frazerd is trying it with 50:1, which is what we US traders will have to live with.

There is much discussion on this board about how high leverage levels don't help you if you don't know how to trade.  But if you do know how to trade, higher leverage levels let you use more aggressive strategies and if you really really know what you're doing, you'll make more money that way without blowing your account.

My move toward the package of tactics we call Phantom_AddSix is with 50:1 in mind.  To do well with that leverage level, we have to be extremely efficient and pretty doggone sophisticated.  And we still have to stand ready to adjust to further changes in the terms dictated to small account retail traders.
