--- 帖子 #1209 ---
MC, you asked me to look at which pairs contribute the most to closing in the phantom EAs. I have put together some figures for you using only the results from my 500:1 Phantom14_Add_02-taz. I used that one because it has, by far, the most trades and most closings.

The results are very interesting. I looked only at the biggest winner and 2nd biggest winner of each closing and, since this is a taz EA, I had to determine whether the trades were RightWay trades or WrongWay.

Of the 88 biggest and 2nd biggest trades, 60 were wrong way trades. That is almost 70% and I think that is significant. Maybe we need to reverse the phantom buys and sells as a first step.

The top 3 BUY contributors were GBPUSD with 7 1st places and 6 2nd places of which 8 were wrong way trades. Next was EURJPY with 6 1st and 5 2nd places of which 5 were wrong way. Third was GBPJPY with 6 1st and 3 2nds of which 8 were wrong way.

The top 3 SELL contributors were EURUSD with 6 1st and 7 2nd places of which 9 were wrong way trades. Next was AUDUSD with 7 1st and 4 2nd places of which 7 were wrong way. Third was GBPCHF with 5 1st and 3 2nd places of which 5 were wrong way.

I hope this will be useful information since I spent a lot of time sifting it out.

--- 帖子 #1217 ---
Hi guys,

It has been a long time since I posted on this forum.  But I have been watching and reading this thread with interest.  I love the concept of the basket trade.  And in particular how you are applying it with the Phantom series of EA's.

I have been trialling the Phantom_Addsix_02 live on a small IBFX mini account and my observations are as follows:

1/  I note that there may be a small bug - I am currently getting two pairs open on the hour sometimes, both on the same side of the hedge (G/U and E/J).  This has occurred several times, but not every hour when one or the other has opened.  Also commented on by Vienna.

2/  I think it is destablizing to the trade pattern (I am not referring to the basket hedge) when a large move is made in a single pair between the hourly check by the EA for the biggest winning pair.  So for example Cable moved up rapidly over 1300/1400 GMT yesterday (20th Oct) - this meant that the EA is taking only trades on this pair but it has missed all the big move up (intra hour action).  It then starts taking trades, even though the price action is pulling back and all the existing cable trades are currently negative.  I believe Frazerd alluded to this also.

With a very large move on one pair within the six tradable pairs if there is a subsequent and sustained pull back we may find the EA going into some level of drawdown before the other side of the hedge is able to counter balance - since it is forced to only trade that pair until it gets a pair from the other side of the hedge to become the biggest winning pair (but I guess this will depend on your initial risk plan).

Possible solution:  have the EA check every 15 minutes and trade 1/4 size contracts for similar margin and spread risk.  Also have the EA only add positions when all previous positions are profitable only (as in some of the other versions), this is less likely to negatively impact the results as the EA would be checking every 15 minutes.  The dd will also be contained as a result.

I guess there is nothing really new in my comments - but felt it worth summarising and the fact that others have touched on these points also.  I am not a programmer, so am limited to observations.

I think you guys are doing an excellent job - love the effort and the energy.

Tim

--- 帖子 #1228 ---
regarding the bug you mentioned, its not a bug, i checked the code. at the top of the hour it places order for the biggest phantom winner. just one symbol only. it doesnt order a 'hedge' pair. so when you start the EA, initailly you may have only one order. and after 1 hr you may have order on same or a different pair. if its same pair then you are building dependancy on that pair, but good news is its biggest phantom winner. after a while you may have a basket of trades with 1 or 2 or 3 or more pairs.

there is no guarantee that hedge is built here. thats why i always place a stoploss of 200 pips just in case.

the reasn why you see 2 trades on the hour sometimes is, the hour check goes for a full minute, 00 to 59 sec, so during this 60 sec you may have one pair as biggest winner and again another pair as biggest winner. then it places orders for all these pairs. but thats rare

i agree with you on checking more frequently. may be every 15 min or 30  min. also about adding only if all its previous adds are in profit. otherwise theres no use , you are just adding spreads to your PL. more orders, more pips to beat the spread

--- 帖子 #1235 ---
The EA only places trades when a phantom pair is +20 or -20 pips or more. Your first screen shot shows only 1 pair at 20 pips, but if it was not at 20 at the hour or half hour when the EA checks, it would not open a trade. The second shot shows no phantoms - or + 20 pips. That is the reason there are no trades.

Also, be aware that every time you make a change and click OK on the input menu, it resets the pip count back to zero. So if you have looked at it and not made changes, be sure to click Cancel rather than OK. Cancel will not reset to zero.

--- 帖子 #1236 ---
Hi Caillou,

The problem could be due to lot size. At line 667, lot size is calculated to have 2 decimal places, your MT4 may not be able to trade lot size with 2 decimal places, eg. 0.12. Try changing the code to only produce 1 decimal place to see if it trades.

Line 667:

UseLots = StrToDouble(DoubleToStr(UseLots,2));

change to,

UseLots = StrToDouble(DoubleToStr(UseLots,1));

Sorry if I'm wrong, I'm just trying to help.

Good luck.

--- 帖子 #1241 ---
Some of you are expressing concern that the hedge is not being reliably constructed via real trades.

With Phantom_AddSix_02, it should be more of a concern than with 01.

With Phantom_AddSix_01, all that's required to open a trade on a pair is for its phantom trade to be positive.

However, with ver 02, a pair must have distinguished itself as a biggest phantom winner among all 14 pairs before it will be traded.  No, I'm not going to whittle down to tracking only the 6 pairs.  It seems to me that we shouldn't be worried about trading the other side of the hedge until some of those pairs move strongly enough to distinguish themselves as biggest winners among the larger basket.  When my theory is proven wrong, I'll come up with EAs that deal with it.

I have not tried to make myself the policeman over the noise occurring on the thread, but there is quite a bit.  The main reason I don't is because it's not my place to do it.  Also, traders can learn from seeing theories put to the test.  We all like the freedom to test our ideas openly.  I have strong opinions so when I express them I hope they don't discourage a free exchange of ideas.

Yes I feel you should at least try mightily to figure out how to code an idea if you believe in it.  If you think the idea could make you into a millionaire, why wouldn't you invest the blood, sweat and tears into mastering this little MQ4 programming language?  I know it's not easy but I deeply respect those who at least try.  Frazerd earned my utmost respect through his coding efforts and through his relentless objective analysis of trading results.  I ponder his suggestions carefully since I know he spends much time observing, thinking and sharing his analysis.

It's easy to ask me to implement your ideas but I do my own independent thinking based mostly on data (trading statements) presented on the thread, and only rarely based on someone's suggestions.

______

Next topic -- getting the settings right.

I'm a US trader so I'm stuck with US brokers.  I test with 50:1 leverage.

Based on statements I'm seeing, including my own, I'm going to start using

0.67 for MaxMarginToUse and 1.0 for ProfitPct.  This applies only the the NON-taz Phantom_AddSix EAs.

If I run out of margin with those settings, I'll adjust those two settings downward, proportionally, until my margin is staying safe -- 500% or better is nice.

I'd probably adjust the settings downward as follows.

MaxMarginToUse at 0.335  and ProfitPct at 0.5

MaxMarginToUse at 0.1675 and ProfitPct at 0.25

You may want to try other values but what I'm suggesting is to keep the MaxMarginToUse / ProfitPct ratio at about 0.67.

--- 帖子 #1258 ---
Here is a new version of Phantom_AddSix.

It has a subtle change from version 02 in an attempt to make it a little more like version 01, yet more efficient than that version. And it won't have the limitation that the biggest winning phantom must be biggest among all 14 pairs as in version 02.

Instead, a winning phantom must only be the largest among the six traded pairs in order for a trade to be opened. In other words, we limit the biggest phantom winner candidates to EURCHF, EURJPY, CHFJPY, GBPCHF, GBPUSD, USDCHF.

This means that as soon as any of these six pairs become positive phantoms, we will trade them during minute 0. We don't have to wait for them to distinguish themselves among all 14 pairs.

With version 03, it is possible that more than one trade can be opened in minute 0, but less likely than in version 01.

I believe this makes ver 03 a true hybrid of 01 and 02. I won't pretend this is all my idea since I think there was at least one suggestion along these lines. There is still "baggage" code for the other 8 pairs in the EA, but it won't hurt anything. If this EA is successful, I'll trim it later.

Note that MaxMarginToUse is defaulted at 0.67 and ProfitPct is at 1.0. If this is too aggressive for 50:1 accounts, we'll crank these settings down proportionally, e.g., 0.335 and 0.5 or whatever makes sense.

Version 03a is exactly the same as version 03, but it only allows one pair to be traded during minute 0.

Version 03b is exactly the same as version 03a, but it resets the phantom trades every 8 hours, roughly in synch with the 3 major market opening times (Asian, Euro/UK Zone, USA).

|

v

--- 帖子 #1316 ---
I found my demo went into a sequeunce that was impossible to recover from with the Taz version 02.  Since all the pairs went in one direction placing correct direction trades for 7 pairs and reversed direction trades for six of the other 7 pairs.  Then the market completely moved back the other direction and left all the pairs (bar one) stranded.  As a result the EA could never get out of the DD situation unless the market reversed back to the original direction.

So MC is right in that it moves outside the bounds of the hedge.

Larger lot sizes or a smaller percent target simply mask this situation for longer by getting you to your target percent more quickly.  But I would imagine all combinations will get caught out as my demo did at some stage.  (I shut it down with a 35% DD to restart with other versions).

I think the Taz version will work if it simply takes the trades over the +20 pip threshold (or what ever we set), but only for that direction - and no reverse direction trades for -20 pip threshold.  In this way the EA will recover with the other side of the hedge if price action reverses.  I can't remember if this variation has been built before....

Tim

--- 帖子 #1317 ---
This is an interesting idea.  Invariably we go into some sort of DD each time pairs are opened up.  I have never seen a sequence open up and go straight into profit.  Obviously we have the initial negative situation of the spreads to overcome,  but these aside there is almost always a level of DD associated to each equity pop that is often as large as the target percent (or bigger).

I would be keen to test a version like this roundrock.  I would run it at an entry at -0.5% DD with a 0.5% normal target percent.

I you can post your version i would be keen to test it also.

Thanks

Tim

--- 帖子 #1325 ---
D*mn, typed an answer. But clicked the close tab cross instead of switching to the other tab.....

Again, but shorter:

@ Boki. Not sure if it can be done easily. The EA looks at the balance info to determine the amount of profit. So runnning two EA's (with different magic numbers!!) at one account will base the $profit target on the same info. The EA's need to completely rewritten to change that I guess. But on the otherhand, i'm not a programmer. Maybe somebody can implement your idea.

@ Aajduk: It is possible. Depends on when you started the EA's.

The normal versions are kind of hedged by the devide in a BUY group of 7 pairs and a SELL group of 7 pairs. See first post, second link.

The .taz versions BUY and SELL BOTH groups. That's why Metacoder warned us that the hedging-safety isnt in the .taz versions.

The .taz versions can make a lot of profit in a short time, but also a lot of loss. Drawdown can go to 25% and higher. The normal versions are lower in max drawdown (app. 15%) , in my experience.

The Addsix-versions open only 6 different pairs instead of 14.

If you want to search for the description of a version, click on the paperclip in right corner. Click "hide images", search the mq4 file of the version you want info on and then click on the post to read it.

Or click on "Metacoder" Look under "internet activity" and click on posts to quickscan all his posts. Just search a bit and all the info can be found

--- 帖子 #1327 ---
This is because the taz versions trade outside of the defined synthetic hedge. They can make profit fast but can also take your account into drawdown from which it might not recover.

One like Phantom_Addsix_03b stays within the defined synthetic hedge and may not be as thrilling but is also much less likely to get your account into a hole it can't climb out of.

--- 帖子 #1335 ---
New Twist        they write:

Initially, buy the phantom-buy group of pairs and sell the phantom-sell group of pairs.

Every hour, add a trade to the phantom pair that is the biggest phantom  winner. Also add a reverse trade to the phantom pair that is the biggest  phantom loser. Before adding any trades, require that no trades exist  on the pair, or that all preexisting trades on the biggest phantom  winner/loser pairs be in profit. There is no symbol marking in this  version as it is redundant with the check for preexisting trades being  in profit.

Close reverse/"wrong-way" trades if they hit one-tenth of DollarProfitTarget. This is the "gravy" profit.

Let me know if it doesn't appear to be trading as intended, there's a brand new function called TakeWrongwayProfit.

this ea is your ea -allright?

please can you the ea setup for this:

Instead, a winning phantom must only be the largest among the six traded  pairs in order for a trade to be opened. In other words, we limit the  biggest phantom winner candidates to EURCHF, EURJPY, CHFJPY, GBPCHF,  GBPUSD, USDCHF.

--- 帖子 #1344 ---
A short amount of time with any strategy isn't a good indication of what it will do in all market conditions (obviously).  When a taz version gets caught with a lot of open trades during a sharp reversal, you'll see the downside of it.

Also you could have different settings on the different EAs. Are the lot sizes the same?

--- 帖子 #1345 ---
With the taz versions and some of the other EAs, it might be worthwhile to put the following code at the start of the AddIfNeeded function:

Inserted Code
if MathMod(TimeHour(TimeCurrent()),8) == 0.0 &&
TimeMinute(TimeCurrent()) == 1)
{
ResetPhantoms();
}

This resets the phantom trades every 8 hours.  The advantage of this is that we catch changes in market direction sooner.

--- 帖子 #1346 ---
there is a typo in there, unbalanced brackets, try this

if (MathMod(TimeHour(TimeCurrent()),8) == 0.0 &&

TimeMinute(TimeCurrent()) == 1)

{

ResetPhantoms();

}

--- 帖子 #1369 ---
MaxMarginToUse at 0.335 and ProfitPct at 0.5, or something along those lines, might be about right for 50:1 leverage.

Note that some of the versions are more conservative in how many trades they add, so that possibly we could get away with more aggressive settings.

Frazer's reporting is so critical because it gives us good data for making these decisions.

--- 帖子 #1370 ---
I took some time to study Frazer's latest spreadsheet. What I saw was pretty much what I expected.

Add_02-taz has the unhedged problem and AddSix_01 simply adds too many trades.

AddSix_02 is more efficient and Frazer's adjustment of MaxMarginToUse to 0.4 might continue working well.

AddSix_03, 03a and 03b are trading as I'd expect and I do think the 0.67 setting for MaxMarginToUse might be too high.

The following settings might be more prudent:

MaxMarginToUse: 0.4

ProfitPct: 1.0

MaxMarginToUse: 0.335

ProfitPct: 0.5

Somewhere in that range of MaxMarginToUse/ProfitPct proportionality (0.4 to 0.67) lies the sweet spot for 50:1 leveraged trading.

And I still think aiming for minimum margin levels of around 500% is good.

--- 帖子 #1403 ---
-If it resets, it only resets the values for the PHANTOM trades. Time will tell if this is a good implementation or not.

-VPS is a Virtual Private Server. You rent harddiskspace from a company with fast computers and a fast and reliable internet connection. You can run MT4 with EA's 24/7 there and you don't have to let your own home computer on all the time. You can access the VPS with MT4 trough the internet or with remote desktop I believe.

--- 帖子 #1420 ---
Here is a solution to the lotstep issue we see with certain brökers. I think this will work but I haven't tested it for myself yet; please be sure to do so.

First, in the Internal Variables section of the EA, declare the variable LotStep as

double LotStep;

Then in the GetAccountInfo function we need the following statement:

LotStep = MarketInfo(Symbol(), MODE_LOTSTEP);

The SetLotSize function needs to have these lines in it:

UseLots = valLastFlatEq * Investment * (Leverage / MarketInfo(Symbol(), MODE_LOTSIZE));
UseLots = StrToDouble(DoubleToStr(UseLots/LotStep,0))*LotStep;
UseLots = StrToDouble(DoubleToStr(UseLots,2));

That last line may not be necessary, but we'll keep it if we need to change number of lot size digits for odd-duck brökers.

Here's a copy of Phantom_AddSix_03b that has the lotstep fix in it.

|

v

--- 帖子 #1421 ---

On that note, any idea whether it will be rounding down or up?

For example, if my mmtu setting calculates the lotsize to trade at .09, is it going to round down to .05, or up to .10?

If ea calculates lotsize to trade at .14, is it going to round down to .10 or up to .15?

--- 帖子 #1422 ---
It'll round down because the 0 in the call DoubleToStr(UseLots/LotStep,0) eliminates the fractional portion, leaving us with a whole number (integer) to multiply times LotStep.

See this is why you guys pay me the big bucks.

--- 帖子 #1435 ---
It's possible, but we don't depend on that to make our money.  The pairs do all kinds of things at different times.  But always some pairs are moving more than the others. We identify which ones those are and trade them.  Pretty simple.

One of the beautiful things about a many-pair synthetic hedge is that all components of one side of the hedge DO NOT move together in the same direction.

--- 帖子 #1436 ---
Now let's not outsmart ourselves.  In a strongly directional market, this would be a surefire way to get into big drawdown, fast.

And if we try to outsmart ourselves even further by trying to "detect" that we're in a sideways market so maybe we should trade opposite the normal direction, we should remind ourselves that market action can suddently break out into strong directional movement at any moment, right after we've opened a batch of "sideways trades".

--- 帖子 #1437 ---
Resetting the phantom trades near the opening time of each of the three major global trading regions somewhat mimics the effect of opening different instances of the EA at those same times.

--- 帖子 #1438 ---
Yes, not cutting the losers is a key difference with the phantoms, plus letting pairs distinquish themselves with the phantom trade technique before we open actual trades.

--- 帖子 #1443 ---
A little idea:

To prevent getting chopped up in sideways markets or getting into a trade too early, use a dollar buffer amount between the 1st and 2nd biggest winners.

E.g. Dollar Buffer = $1.00

1st BW = $0.86

2nd BW = $0.45

NO TRADE

...

1st BW = $1.97

2nd BW = $0.51

TRADE THE 1st BW

--- 帖子 #1444 ---
poltroni, you can start the 03b EA anytime.  But it does depend on your broker server's GMT setting though.

--- 帖子 #1469 ---
Lets say the EA starts now. it adds orders for GU, EJ. and after another 1 hr lets say it adds CHFJPY. now these orders are in place. lets say the total loss of these 3 orders after some time reaches 30$ or 1% draw down.  now you are down 1%. as per my mod, dont place these 3 orders. keep them in EA, calcualte the darwdown, when it reaches 1 %, now place these 3 orders. with this you are saving 1%. you can reach the target quicker compared to normal EA. most of the times the draw down reaches atleast 1% before retraces and results in profit

with this you can even increase your profit percentage a little since you entered at discounted price compared to normal EA

--- 帖子 #1488 ---
Saidar and all, reports do not mean anything unless you tell us:

Type of account - Standard or Mini - most will be standard unless trading with IBFX

Leverage

MaxMarginToUse setting

ProfitPct setting

Remember that MC, on most of these EAs, has the default settings designed for a 50:1 mini account. If you are trading at higher leverages and on standard accounts you will need to adjust the settings down.

For example, I am using AddSix_03b on a 500:1 Tadawul standard account using MaxMargin 0.1 and ProfitPct 1.0. It has done pretty well with those settings until this morning. Max DD has gone as low as -17% and Lowest Margin %, which is the most important item in your screen comments, has been down to 993%, which I consider too low for a 500:1 leveraged account. So I will probably set MaxMargin lower and ProfitPct to 0.5 and see how that works out.

The point is that if you are not trading at 50:1 leverage on a IBFX type mini account where 1 pip = 1 centUS ($0.01 US), you need to experiment with different settings until you find what works for your situation.

Also, the latest settings MC has posted for the AddSix EAs at 50:1 leverage is MaxMargin 0.3 and ProfitPct 0.5. The original version was set at 0.67 and 1.0. If you haven't changed those that could also be part of your problem.

--- 帖子 #1523 ---
A theoretical question:

If we are looking at whether "phantom trades are profitable" when they opened at a given time...then isn't that the same as looking at the difference in price between "now" and "then"?

So conceivably, if at any time "now" we could compute "when was the then", we don't need to store and save in global variables the opening of the phantom trades, we just have to compare prices now vs then.

The strategy is a "trend follower" looking at unsmoothed deltas between now (top of every hour) and certain mark points, and opening trades in the pair & direction of the strongest trend.   Real time close happens any time basket profit is sufficiently large.

Is there something I'm missing?

If not, then perhaps the code infrastructure for storage & management of the phantoms are superfluous if one can look up previous prices directly.

--- 帖子 #1527 ---
"On the newest versions which reset every 8 hours won't the start times be nearly always on-the-hour, in which case you could use the the opens of 1H bars as a "then" reference point? "

Since I dont know squat about coding, I guess you are asking if there is an easier way to code the phantoms. That I dont know. But you are correct in that you are looking at difference in price from start of phantoms to the current price. You would have to ask MC but I dont think the phantoms start on begining of one hour bar. They start when you start up the EA or when there is a equity pop. As for the 8 hour reset, Dont know if its the top of the hour or 8 hours from when the EA started.

As for the stategy you are correct, it is very short term trend trading (from start or reset of phantoms).  When it works well you will get a equity pop just about every day or twice a day. The problems arise when the markets get choppy. Thats where the concept of the synthetic hedge comes in. If you have long trades for ex. in EUR/JPY and the market turns short the ea will then probably start to take shorts in CHF/JPY thus somewhat balancing out your exposure. I think the trick is to keep exposure somewhat balanced enough without taking too much drawdown until a few pairs move far enough and long enough to give you an equity pop. At least thats my take on it.

All the testing and new versions now I believe are looking for the best ways to avoid those big drawdowns and get quicker equity pops.

--- 帖子 #1531 ---
I have downloaded and looked the source code and am running it, and I've read a significant part of the thread.

Is this correct (please correct as necessary)

At top of each hour, the bot looks at the difference in price at present vs price of the same pair at the saved mark price (the phantoms).  Those saved prices are stored in MT4 persistent global variables.  The robot computes from all pairs on the list "which one would have been the largest winner", i.e. the hypothetical profit difference assuming a fixed lot size (not sure about) trade would have been entered in each pair.  Half are designated to be always buys and another half always sells. The robot enters a real trade in the same direction and in the same pair which is the one with the greatest win among the hypothetical trades.

When I say "statistic" I'm using it in the technical sense that any concrete function extracted from observations is called a "statistic", i.e. an actual number computed from data as opposed to a parameter of a theoretical unknown distribution. In this case the hypothetical profit which is a multiplicative factor times the price difference is what I call the statistic.

I call it "trend following" because once there is a hypothetical winner, meaning the price has changed in a certain direction by the maximum amount among pairs, it places a trade in the same direction on the same pair under the assumption that the price is more probable to continue in the same direction.  I call this "trend following" because it profits when there are positive autocorrelations in price differences (between now and the phantom---i.e. the market moved in a certain direction, and the now and the future when real trade is active, in the same direction).

--- 帖子 #1532 ---
Well mb, you are obviously a hell of a lot smarter than I. I can hardly pronounce some of the words you use and therefore I have no idea what you are talking about.

The phantom trades are real time trades and yes, half are always buys and the other half sells - they change with every tick of the pair. At the top of each hour the EA looks at the prices of the phantoms, which are shown in your screen comments too, and places a real trade of whatever pair is the biggest winner at that exact moment. Then when the trades come into profit it closes all trades when the equity reaches ProfitPct above Last Flat Equity (the last time all trades were closed).

That, in a nutshell and in my Tennessee hillbilly language, is how the EA works. If that is what you said above, then you have it right.

--- 帖子 #1549 ---
I had the same experience as vienna early this morning on my AddSix_01 demo. On my spread sheet you can see very clearly what happened.

Margin went to 100%, which triggers a margin call. The broker software then closes the biggest losers until margin rises above 100% again. It then waits until margin goes back down to 100% and repeats the closing of losers until it goes back above 100%, etc., etc.

After several of those margin call closes, apparently the GBPUSD and CHFJPY went on a big run in our favor. My demo had 240 open trades at that time. I had set PP at 0.25. It reached 25% profit and started closing trades at 1400 GMT. It took 5 minutes to close the 240 trades and profit just kept increasing as they were closing. My account, which was in a margin call situation ended up with a profit of almost 8%. Amazing.

--- 帖子 #1566 ---
The 14 pairs were suggested by another trader on this forum. An analysis of why it is a pure synthetic hedge is discussed in first post of the Confirm 14 thread - http://www.forexfactory.com/showthread.php?t=251869

Is it MT5 that doesn't have all of the currency pairs, or is it the broker?

You just want to have a balanced many-pair set where the numerators and denominators are the same after cancelling common numerators and denominators.

This illustrates what I'm referring to:

http://members.cox.net/rcochran/supercurrencies.jpg

See how we are left with AUD+EUR+EUR+GBP+NZD / CHF+JPY+JPY+JPY+USD on each side?

If you can readily see the several smaller synthetic hedge combinations inside this larger synthetic hedge, you have the same level of understanding I do in this area.

--- 帖子 #1568 ---
The opposite can happen. Frazer recently got a margin call but ended up with an 8% gain.

It's important to use settings that DON'T let margin calls happen, and to select strategies that, while possibly very boring, do not open too many trades. We want our full closures to be as quick as possible, and fewer trades means quicker closures. This is why I like AddSix_02(a). But then people try it and notice it can take a long time to open a trade, and they get bored/frustrated, and think something is wrong. Lack of understanding and impatience is the root cause. Relentless pursuit of full understanding and patience are the cure.

--- 帖子 #1591 ---
Keep in mind that when reducing the PP from 1% to 0.25%, you are in effect increasing the spread needed to trade by x4 just to get to the equivalent of 1% PP.  Although larger spread spend is a minor issue in the long run.

Reducing MMTU is one way to solve the large DD issue as MetaCoder has pointed out a couple of times already.

Finding the optimum MMTU & PP settings for your own Account size and Leverage are key - just like frazerd has posted through his research.

The benefit of it is that trades are not taken unless a pair is really seeing some strong action. The strategy is less vulnerable to reacting to head-fakes in market action.

--- 帖子 #1628 ---
It's not the reset every 8 hours because my Collective FX and Tadawul accounts are running with EAs that reset the phantoms every 8 hours, and they're doing very well. And I don't even think it's the bigger spreads on IBFX.

I believe it's the proportion of lot size to ProfitPct.

Since my Collective FX and Tadawul accounts are standard accounts with small $3,000 balances, each tick is worth more money than a tick on the 50:1 IBFX accounts. While the dollar profit targets are the same, they are reached faster.

To imitate this on 50:1 IBFX accounts, we'd need to ratchet the ProfitPct down proportionally. I haven't done the math to figure out what the value would be.

If we reduce the ProfitPct on the IBFX accounts, each full closure would be for a pretty small amount, but I think we'd see more frequent closures with fewer periods of a lot of trades staying open for a relatively long time.

--- 帖子 #1629 ---

It's looking to me like pretty small profit targets are appropriate. Exactly how small, I'm not sure. And then we need to understand how to proportion everything, considering account type, leverage level, etc.

Like many of you, I want an EA I can drag on drop on just about ANY MT4 platform and not have to worry about all of these settings.

--- 帖子 #1649 ---
This is same as Phantom_AddSix_02 except it will start the basket only after reaching a minimum drawdown level. Several times we see the regular EA reaching a drawdown level of 1% or 2% before reaching profit percentage. with this EA we dont enter strautaway.

Lets say the EA is started, at every hour it finds the biggest phantom winner from 14 and if its one of our 6 then it adds this to a buffer. It doesnt send to broker yet. Like this it keeps adding to buffer every hour based on same condition. The EA keeps calculating the PL of the buffer. If the buffer loss is 1.5% (configurable as MinDrawdownToEnter)

, then it will release these buffered orders to broker at current market price. Because of this we are ahead of 1.5% when compared to those that are trading regular Phantom_AddSix_02.

since we are ahead by 1.5%, we will reach the profit quicker than regular guys. we can aim higher profit compared to regular EA. we can increase the PP by 20% ie from 1% to 1.2% or from 0.5% to 0.6%

if the buffer profit reaches PP without reaching MinDrawdownToEnter, then it will close the buffer and starts again. ofcourse we are missing a winning trade compared to regular EA.

Advantage with this : Lower DD. higher PP on each cycle

Disadvantage : we may miss some profitable cycles if it happens too quickly

Settings : MinDrawdownToEnter. this is the only new parameter added. if this is too low, then you dont get much benefit in terms of DD. If its too high, you miss some profitable trades. I would suggest 1%-1.5% to start with. dont forget to increase your PP. if this is 0, then its exactly same as reguar Phantom_AddSix_02. since we have the buffer, this may look slow in terms of trades. it may take a while to see the first trade in your account

--- 帖子 #1655 ---
Account History Tab

Information about all trade  operations performed is stored in the "Account History" tab. The entire history  is displayed as a table with the following fields (from left to right):  Order — operation ticket number. It is the unique number of a trade  operation;  Time — time of position opening. It is given in YYYY.MM.DD HH:MM  (year.month.day hour:minute) format. This is the time when the position was  opened;  Type — trade operation type. Only three types of trade operations can  be found here: "Balance" — entering of funds in the account, "Buy" — a long  position, and "Sell" — a short position;  Lots — amount of lots participated in the operation;  Symbol — this field shows the name of the security participated in the  operation;  Price — price of position opening. This is the price at which the  position was opened;  S/L — level of the Stop Loss order placed.  If a trade position was closed by this order, its corresponding cell will be  colored in red, and "[s/l]" will appear in the field of comments. If no order  was placed, zero value will appear in this field. On the other hand, if the an  order was placed, but did not trigger, its value will still be shown in this  field. At that, the cell will not be colored, and no "[s/l]" will be output in  the field of comments. More details about working with orders are given in the  corresponding section;  T/P — level of the Take Profit order  placed. If a trade position was closed by this order, its corresponding cell  will be colored in green, and "[t/p]" will appear in the field of comments. If  no order was placed, zero value will appear in this field. On the other hand, if  the an order was placed, but did not trigger, its value will still be shown in  this field. At that, the cell will not be colored, and no "[t/p]" will be output  in the field of comments. More details about working with orders are given in  the corresponding section;  Time — time of position closing. It is given in YYYY.MM.DD HH:MM  (year.month.day hour:minute) format. This is the time when the position was  closed;  Price — price of position closing. This is the price at which the  position was closed;  Commission — commissions charged by the brokerage company when trade  operations are performed will be stored in this field;  Swap — the swaps charged are stored in this field;  Profit — the financial result of transaction will be written in this  field. Positive number means that the transaction was profitable, and the  negative one does vice versa. The profit is shown only in the deposit currency  here, unlike it is in the field of the same name in the "Trade" tab.  Comments — comments on trade operations are stored in this column. A  comment can be input only at opening of a position or placing an order. The  comment cannot be changed when an order or a position are being modified.  Besides, a comment to the trade operation can be input by the brokerage  company.  Context Menu

Commands allowing to manage the history range and  data performance, as well as commands of history data export are grouped in the  context menu:   All History — show the entire account history. At this command  execution, the whole financial history of the account will appear in the screen  without any limitations by time;  Last 3 Months — show only the last 3-months history;  Last Month — show only the last month history;  Custom Period — show history for the selected period. At this command  execution, the window that manages the history range will appear where one can  select one of the pre-defined ranges (the "Period" field) or specify them  manually in the fields of "From" and "to";  Save as Report — save the account history as a HTML file. At that, a  window allowing to select a path for saving of the file will appear;  Save as Detailed Report — save the account history as a HTML file. A  detailed report differs from a normal one for an additional set of parameters.  After this command has been executed, a window allowing to select a path for  saving the file will appear;  Commissions — show/hide the "Commissions" column;  Comments — show/hide the "Comments" column. Comments to trade  operations are stored in this column. A comment can only be input at opening of  a position or at placing of an order. Besides, the brokerage company can write a  comment to the trade operation, as well;  Auto Arrange — automatic arrangement of column sizes at changing of  the window size;  Grid — show/hide grid for separating of columns. best regards

vienna

Open Account history tab. (somewhere under in the screen of mt4)

Select the period you want the history/statement for (see Vienna's post above)

Right click somewhere on the closed transactions in history tab and select "save as detailled statement" (or something like that. I've a dutch version)

The statement will be openend in your internetbrowser.

--- 帖子 #1669 ---
When he posted that EA, he explained it.

If you put any number except 0, it does not place a real trade until there has been a draw down equal to the percent you specified. It holds the initial trades and tracks their draw down. They become another set of phantom trades. That is why he calls it Phantom.....phantom.

MaxMarginToUse is the percent of your account balance that will be used for each trade. So saider's lot size depends on his account balance.

Most of us do not use that high MMTU, especially if trading higher leverage than 50:1.

--- 帖子 #1684 ---
MetaCoder & roundrock,

Please review the following coding.  What I'm trying to do is prevent over/early trading on a Biggest Phantom Winner.

It's from the AddIfNeeded() function:

(Before this peice of code, I'm actually checking for the first minute of the hour so that the below mods will work - not on the hour)

Inserted Code for (i = Pair1idx; i <= Pair6idx; i++)
{
if (SymbolArray[i] == BiggestPhantomWinnerSymbol &&
AllSymbolTradesInProfit(SymbolArray[i]) &&
!SymbolMarked(SymbolArray[i]))
{
if (i < 3)
{
if (iHigh(SymbolArray[i], PERIOD_M5, 2) > iHigh(SymbolArray[i], PERIOD_M5, 3) && // Check last 15 minutes trend continuation
iHigh(SymbolArray[i], PERIOD_M5, 1) > iHigh(SymbolArray[i], PERIOD_M5, 2) && // Check last 10 minutes trend continuation
MarketInfo(SymbolArray[i], MODE_ASK) > iHigh(SymbolArray[i], PERIOD_M5, 1) && // Last 5 minutes Ask Check for BUYS
iClose(SymbolArray[i], PERIOD_M5, 1) > iHigh(SymbolArray[i], PERIOD_M5, iHighest(SymbolArray[i], PERIOD_M5, MODE_HIGH, 23, 2)))
// Check for 2 hour range breakout
{
Comment("Adding a " + SymbolArray[i] + " buy trade...");
Print("Adding a " + SymbolArray[i] + " long.");
Ticket = OrderSend(SymbolArray[i],OP_BUY,UseLots,MarketInfo(SymbolArray[i], MODE_ASK),
Slippage,0,0,NULL,MagicNumber,Blue);
if (Ticket > 0) MarkSymbolAdded(SymbolArray[i]);
Sleep(100);
}
}
else
// if (i >= 3)
{
if (iLow(SymbolArray[i], PERIOD_M5, 2) < iLow(SymbolArray[i], PERIOD_M5, 3) && // Check last 15 minutes trend continuation
iLow(SymbolArray[i], PERIOD_M5, 1) < iLow(SymbolArray[i], PERIOD_M5, 2) && // Check last 10 minutes trend continuation
MarketInfo(SymbolArray[i], MODE_BID) < iLow(SymbolArray[i], PERIOD_M5, 1) && // Last 5 minutes Bid Check for SELLS
iClose(SymbolArray[i], PERIOD_M5, 1) < iLow(SymbolArray[i], PERIOD_M5, iLowest(SymbolArray[i], PERIOD_M5, MODE_LOW, 23, 2)))
// Check for 2 hour range breakout
{
Comment("Adding a " + SymbolArray[i] + " sell trade...");
Print("Adding a " + SymbolArray[i] + " short.");
Ticket = OrderSend(SymbolArray[i],OP_SELL,UseLots,MarketInfo(SymbolArray[i], MODE_BID),
Slippage,0,0,NULL,MagicNumber,Red);
if (Ticket > 0) MarkSymbolAdded(SymbolArray[i]);
Sleep(100);
}
}
}
}

Do you guys think it will work?

Do I have the Ask and bid checks the right way around?

Why did I choose a 2 hour range breakout?  I have no idea... I guess I doubled the "Every hour" bit and went with it.

Cheers,

the-game.

--- 帖子 #1695 ---
Why is the lot size such an issue for you?

He was obviously just tweaking the MMTU setting for his own needs (Last flat equity/Leverage/Account type).

Here's how MetaCoder calculates the lot size:

(MMTU / 100) * Last flat equity * (Leverage / Account Lotsize)

Where Account Lotsize can usually either be:

100000 units on a STANDARD account

or

10000 units on a MINI account

Last flat equity is basically your balance before the EA placed any trades / after the EA closed the trades

hi frazer, as usual excellent reports. lot of insight into how the EA works with various settings

one question. on reducing PP to 0.25 with same MMTU 0.4, you mentioned it will reduce DD

my understanding is DD is a function of lotsize and number of open trades. if we have more open trades, the DD increases. once the basket starts in negative and keep adding same pair again and again and the basket goes in big DD, then it doesnt matter whether PP was 0.25 or 0.5 or 1. only when basket comes into positive territory the PP comes into picture. other scenario would be basket is in positive but unable to reach PP and then goes to negative and DD. but such scenarios are less compared to previous scenario

so my understanding is we need NOT reduce PP for same MMTU. this may not help us in reducing DD in most cases. so why sacrifice PP ?

i still think adding same pair again and again consequitively is the root cause for bigger DD scenario, if we cap that to 3 or 4 then we may solve this issue to some extent without effecting the profitabality. dont add same pair 4th time if all last 3 adds are from same pair and combined PL of the last 3 is in negative.

just my opinion. i will spend some time to add this to the code and see how it works. its not a big change in code

--- 帖子 #1702 ---
Well, I have a different opinion. You will notice that since reducing PP on my demos, they close with fewer trades. Sometimes the EA will come into profit a few dollars and then reverse and go back into a DD situation and that causes more trades to close. Also, unless there is a very strong move, it can take a good deal of time for the trades to get from .25% to .5% profit, during which time more trades are added. So, what I am seeing is that the EAs close much quicker and with significantly fewer trades with PP .25 and therefore less DD.

I partially agree with you on this point, but MC doesn't. EDIT: I think we should not continue to add trades to a winner that has already reversed.

Back before the AddSix EAs, the-game asked for a modification to the Phantom14_Add series that would prevent the EA from adding trades on a pair that is still a biggest winner, but had changed direction and is now becoming a loser. MC came up with Phantom14_Add_02, which adds a trade of the biggest winner only if all previous trades on the pair are winners. That prevents a winner that has reversed and is now heading the wrong way from being added again.

I was seeing a lot of those repetitive pair losers in the AddSix 01 EA, so I extracted the appropriate code from Phantom14_Add_02 and inserted it into AddSix_01 and called it 01x.

I loaded that mod on my AddSix_01 demo Sunday 7 Nov. It already had a bunch of repeat loser trades. It did not add any more trades on those pairs and closed this morning. There is no way to know for sure if the mod had anything to do with that, but I'd like to think it did. We will see what happens going forward.

In any event, AddSix_01 accumulates a LOT of trades because it adds trades of any winning pair every hour. Anything that limits the number of trades, even a little bit has to help.

Here is my modified AddSix_01x and my spreadsheet showing what happened to the last batch of trades on that demo.

--- 帖子 #1763 ---
Hi everyone,

I want to share some thoughts because I really don´t know if I´m right or not.

1.- Manual Intervention: we have recently in the thread some suggestions about setting a start time to run the ea (London Open, NY Open,...), or an end time (NY close), .... I think we have to give the EA a chance to recovery from any big market movement because if not, the next step will be avoid weekend gaps, or big news. We have a perfect syntetic hedge here and sooner or later, recovery will arrive.

2.- The PP factor: maybe I´m wrong but if any basket opened by the EA is able to reach for example a -9.5% DD, then it would be able to reach the same profit, +9.5%. If in my demos all baskets always have gone to at least -1.5% DD, then a 1.0% of PP must be easy to reach.

In my opinion the analysis of the DD is where I´m going to focus all my time and effort.

3.- Maximum DD: again I might be wrong but with a perfect syntetic hedge, DD will never be unlimited, so the main goal must be to establish the max DD tolerable for each leverage.

Sorry for a so long post but I am convinced that this EA is very profitable in the long term.

--- 帖子 #1764 ---
Good thinking. I just posted in the Ph6 thread about margin calls and a possible lesson learned. I think it might apply here.

When margin level gets below 300% (or some other level we designate) close the biggest loser every hour, as well as adding the biggest winner(s) until the margin goes back above the designated level.

We have seen 2 cases now where a margin call actually helped the EA come into profit by closing biggest losers. Rather than waiting for margin calls, why not close biggest losers at some level above margin call? This level could be a external variable so that each trader could use whatever level he/she is comfortable with.

EDIT: It might even be a satisfactory substitute for those folks who are clamering for a stop loss.

--- 帖子 #1769 ---
The goal is to make it as steady and trouble-free as possible but as we all know the forex market is a wild tiger.

The EAs do not in any way prevent manual overrides by the trader.  In fact that is my suggested recourse for dealing with unwanted margin depletion, if it happens.  I could never ever please everyone if I started baking in bailout mechanisms.  Everyone wants something different, so I leave it to each individual to expand on the code, or use another party's code, or use manual measures to deal with any adverse situations.

I concentrate on building reliable software that is better than most manual traders at making money and I hope that's enough.

--- 帖子 #1770 ---
While our latest generation of EAs is able to do well for longer periods than any prior (as far as I know), the black swans are out there.  The market does so many kinds of crazy gyrations at times that I just can't say if we'll ever get an EA that's GUARANTEED to ALWAYS kick out profit with no margin issues.

But we HAVE been successful at extending the amount of time our EAs can thrive, in a wide variety of trending and choppy action.  I'm pleased with our progress to say the least.

--- 帖子 #1779 ---
one quick feedback on going with hourly  trend is it will NOT guarantee you the synthetic hedge and hence can get margin call theoritically

in the current versions of EAs, we always BUY certain pairs and always SELL certain other pairs, so this constitutes a synthetic hedge. now if we go as per ema, we may end up all 6 pairs in LONG and after sometime market may reverse and you get into huge DD

if you mean to say dont change the direction (BUY/SELL), only a additional condition for ema then sythetic hedge will not be disturbed but you may not reach PP quickly as there will be very few trades and there is no guarantee that trend will remain intact for the day. things could change

with x factor the DD issue is addressed to some extent.

with lesser PP (may be 0.5) we can close the basket quickly

just my 2c

--- 帖子 #1780 ---
if you dig this thread there was a discussion on this 3 pair issue. currently we trade 6 pairs EURCHF, EURJPY, CHFJPY, GBPCHF, GBPUSD, USDCHF

so we have EUR, USD, JPY, CHF, GBP so if there is a push in any of these currencies we get to PP. so chances are better with 5 pairs. if you take only 3 pairs you are depending on EUR, USD to privide you that push. so less chances. aslo with 5 pairs we cover all three regions AS, EU, US. so any time of the day we may get push from any of these 5 pairs. with EUR, GBP its almost sure to be dead in AS. so if you trade 3 pairs then do it only in EU, US times.

but you can also argue with more pairs, some will be laggards and will be dragging the basket down always regardless how strong one or two pairs are !!!  thats why its difficult to say which is better.

may be you can have 1 EA to trade ASIA times with asia pairs like JPY, AUD, NZD and 1 EA for EU to cover EUR, GBP, CHF and 1 in US for USD, CAD

but the MC EA has covered all regions all pairs, so it works well overall

--- 帖子 #1787 ---
It depends on what the intent is. My suggestion was based on observing how the margin call can work for us occassionally, rather than against us. My intent would be to boost a low margin back to an acceptable level to give the EA a chance to reach the profit target. Trimming the BIGGEST loser would be the best solution for that. If you only close smallest losers it will probably take a long time to get back to the desired margin level. It might not ever get there. Additionally, in the event that the pair should reverse and become a winner again, which trade would come back into profit quicker and which would remain a loser longer. If we decide to revisit trimming losers on a limited basis, it only makes sense to me to chop the biggest one.

I say "revisit" because MC and I did test a tactic of trimming losers back some time ago, but we were using that as our primary means of getting into profit and closing losers every hour. EDIT: It did not work out well at all. What I'm suggesting now is a very limited use of closing losers to keep an acceptable margin level.

--- 帖子 #1788 ---
Here is an extract of my AddSix_01 spreadsheet with some comments in the margin. It illustrates what I am talking about. There were 240(+) trades in this basket before it dipped below 100% and triggered the first magin call at 12:07 on 1 Nov. It closed a $17 loser and that pushed the margin back above 100% for a short time. Then at 12:10 the margin was below 100% again and it closed a $15 loser and at 12:22 a $14 loser. Finally after 6 Margin call closes over a 30 minute time span, the market started to move in my favor and by 1400 the profit target was reached and the EA began a close-all function which took 5 minutes to close the 240 remaining trades. When the smoke cleared I had a $289 profit.

So what I propose is that we pre-empt the margin call by not letting our margin reach that level. We start closing biggest losers at a user defined margin level and we close them on a scheduled basis, the same schedule we add winners and do it until the desired margin level is regained. That buys us time to let the EA work its way back into profit without experiencing a margin call.

O ye, this is more clear to me, you are right, your idea is better--remove biggest losers.

then i think that a hard-stoploss for each pair seems an OK idea.  then i understand that a hard-stoploss (say, 100 pips) is not a popular idea to many. then how about this idea:

ratio = negative floating pips of a pair / last day move;

or

ratio = negative floating pips of a pair / this pair's profit in the rank;

when 'ratio' is reaching a threshold value, cut its biggest loser.

the logic behind is that the immediate recent price move of this pair is sufficient proof that the price reversed (the profit ranking is no longer valid.) so we exit.

anyway, the way is no better than manual intervening. but it can be coded into the EA.

forgive my dumbness, if i misunderstand the EA's logic...

--- 帖子 #1791 ---
Attached is the original Phantom_AddSix_01x with a reset function similar to 03b, but will just reset once a day.

Choose an hour and set it against the variable "ResetHour".

The EA will reset the Phantoms on that hour on minute 1.

e.g. Just before the London Open like someone had suggested.

Also for those who want to keep the Phantoms "alive" (i.e. Not reset) after you either - Change a setting / Close then open the MT4 platform / Restart your computer (the attached has this so you can refer to that if you get lost)...

1) ...move the SetSymbols(); function call from inside the start() function, into the first line of the init() function

2) ...remove the ResetPhantoms(); function call from inside the init() function

3) ...then you can add the following code in SetGlobalVariableNames()

Inserted Code   strGBPUSDask = MagicNumber+"_"+GBPUSDsym;
strEURGBPask = MagicNumber+"_"+EURGBPsym;
strGBPJPYask = MagicNumber+"_"+GBPJPYsym;
strUSDCHFask = MagicNumber+"_"+USDCHFsym;
strNZDUSDask = MagicNumber+"_"+NZDUSDsym;
strAUDJPYask = MagicNumber+"_"+AUDJPYsym;
strEURJPYask = MagicNumber+"_"+EURJPYsym;

strEURUSDbid = MagicNumber+"_"+EURUSDsym;
strUSDJPYbid = MagicNumber+"_"+USDJPYsym;
strAUDUSDbid = MagicNumber+"_"+AUDUSDsym;
strNZDJPYbid = MagicNumber+"_"+NZDJPYsym;
strGBPCHFbid = MagicNumber+"_"+GBPCHFsym;
strCHFJPYbid = MagicNumber+"_"+CHFJPYsym;
strEURCHFbid = MagicNumber+"_"+EURCHFsym;
4) ...and then add the following code in InitGlobalVars()

Inserted Code   if (!GlobalVariableCheck(strGBPUSDask)) GlobalVariableSet(strGBPUSDask, GBPUSDask);
if (!GlobalVariableCheck(strEURGBPask)) GlobalVariableSet(strEURGBPask, EURGBPask);
if (!GlobalVariableCheck(strGBPJPYask)) GlobalVariableSet(strGBPJPYask, GBPJPYask);
if (!GlobalVariableCheck(strUSDCHFask)) GlobalVariableSet(strUSDCHFask, USDCHFask);
if (!GlobalVariableCheck(strNZDUSDask)) GlobalVariableSet(strNZDUSDask, NZDUSDask);
if (!GlobalVariableCheck(strAUDJPYask)) GlobalVariableSet(strAUDJPYask, AUDJPYask);
if (!GlobalVariableCheck(strEURJPYask)) GlobalVariableSet(strEURJPYask, EURJPYask);

if (!GlobalVariableCheck(strEURUSDbid)) GlobalVariableSet(strEURUSDbid, EURUSDbid);
if (!GlobalVariableCheck(strUSDJPYbid)) GlobalVariableSet(strUSDJPYbid, USDJPYbid);
if (!GlobalVariableCheck(strAUDUSDbid)) GlobalVariableSet(strAUDUSDbid, AUDUSDbid);
if (!GlobalVariableCheck(strNZDJPYbid)) GlobalVariableSet(strNZDJPYbid, NZDJPYbid);
if (!GlobalVariableCheck(strGBPCHFbid)) GlobalVariableSet(strGBPCHFbid, GBPCHFbid);
if (!GlobalVariableCheck(strCHFJPYbid)) GlobalVariableSet(strCHFJPYbid, CHFJPYbid);
if (!GlobalVariableCheck(strEURCHFbid)) GlobalVariableSet(strEURCHFbid, EURCHFbid);
5) ...then add the following code to the RefreshGlobalVars() function

Inserted Code   GBPUSDask = GlobalVariableGet(strGBPUSDask);
EURGBPask = GlobalVariableGet(strEURGBPask);
GBPJPYask = GlobalVariableGet(strGBPJPYask);
USDCHFask = GlobalVariableGet(strUSDCHFask);
NZDUSDask = GlobalVariableGet(strNZDUSDask);
AUDJPYask = GlobalVariableGet(strAUDJPYask);
EURJPYask = GlobalVariableGet(strEURJPYask);

EURUSDbid = GlobalVariableGet(strEURUSDbid);
USDJPYbid = GlobalVariableGet(strUSDJPYbid);
AUDUSDbid = GlobalVariableGet(strAUDUSDbid);
NZDJPYbid = GlobalVariableGet(strNZDJPYbid);
GBPCHFbid = GlobalVariableGet(strGBPCHFbid);
CHFJPYbid = GlobalVariableGet(strCHFJPYbid);
EURCHFbid = GlobalVariableGet(strEURCHFbid);

MetaCoder had the rest of the code implemented, just didn't initialise the Global Variables for some reason.

EDIT: The Phantoms will of course reset as usual after closing all real trades for a profit.

--- 帖子 #1808 ---
Well its more of a design question I asked rather than manually closing out. If the EA is designed around your style then yes you shouldn't intervene unless it strays away from what you expect.

I'm saying more in general terms that all you can do in coding the EA is find the best entry.. and from there its really random and hopefully you have the edge in reaching your PP as it takes trades every bar. This is because you only have 3 pairs and one or more will always be positive if they form a hedge. You seem to get 2 trades some bars.. makes sense but your margin may run out since your lot size is big even for 10k account. Although the "adding only to a winner" filter may help. We'll see how it goes.

--- 帖子 #1831 ---
Just an observation with these EAs.

I'm sure most of you who have tested have witnessed this before.

Once a trading "session" takes over 4 hours to complete, the chances are very small for it to recover.

I notice the best sessions are under 4 hours (i.e. fast)

I don't know how to take advantage of this, just putting it out there for the rest of you to think over.

--- 帖子 #1834 ---
The main points we need to address are:

1. Optimal MMTU and PP for your own Account Balance and Account Leverage

2. Take advantage of the best session times.

I think we are closer more than ever with your help Jag.

I was also on another thread started by ES Trader just recently [A simple breakout system] where he actually places his breakout trades just before each Forex session close - not on the session opens.

His reasoning is because the big traders want to "wrap up" their trades before the session ends, hence big market movement at around those times.

We can take advantage of his theory as well as the session opens/overlaps.

--- 帖子 #1840 ---
trading session, leg, what ever you want to call it starts on our first real order through to when all orders are closed.

The 4 hour thing is just a pattern I've seen where after the 4 hours the EA tends to eat up your margin while it is trying to recover.

Basically the EA is trying to adapt to a changing market, but it is hard for it to do so if there are active orders that were adapted to the market more than 4 hours ago.

The only way to know if we can close faster if we start our trading session at the start of each Open or near the Close of the EU, US, AS markets is to test.

I agree with what you are saying about the AS hours, so we should probably concentrate on EU and US hours, just like Jag has proposed.

--- 帖子 #1841 ---

If you look at AS its possible to have a profitable basket either during start of tokyo or between tokyo and start of frankfurt/london.

--- 帖子 #1867 ---
Last time I will post this:

(Account Equity Before EA places REAL TRADES) * (MMTU / 100) * (Leverage / Account Type)

Account Types:

STANDARD = 100,000

MINI = 10,000

So e.g. for you navk

5000 * (0.6 / 100) * (200 / 100000) = 0.06 Lot size

--- 帖子 #1872 ---
Hi Caillou,

I think this is a very good variation on the theme.  I am trading this on a small live account to test it under real conditions.

Two suggstions:

1/  Would you consider having the EA look for new trades every 30minutes rather than at the top of the hour.  Often the price action has run a long way within an hour and the EA misses out on this when only taking trades on the hour - it could make the difference, creating quicker close outs (equity pops).

2/  As the news releases come out mainly on the top of the hour or the half hour - why not have the EA look for trades, say, 10 minutes past the hour (and if you consider having it look for trades every 30 minutes - then it could look at 10 past and 40 minutes past the hour for trades...??)

We could even look at the EA taking trades 10 minutes before the hour and be in trades ahead of any news event...  either way the EA has to run the gauntlet of the news event.

But better to look off the hour so that the trade is not entered with massive slippage.....

cheers.

Also I think some sort of volatility filter could help with killing off the open trades when price swings get too big (after a large number of trades open into one direction) and the trades are in profit, and then the market reverses.  If it gets into profit then this filter could kick in if there is a rapid move back to zero - after say reaching at least ~60% of targeted pp.  Usually once the EA moves into a decent profit it eventually hits the pp.  So closing out at BE after ~60% in the profit may help eliiminate the chance of a bigger DD if it reverses from a good profit position....

Tim

--- 帖子 #1906 ---
It will work well for others who are trading the same leverage, but may not work for different leverages. Also, timing of first entry using new settings can cause a difference in results. I have never figured out exactly why, but 2 people running the same EA with same leverage and same settings may get totally different results. The only difference being start time, would lead you to believe that is the determining factor. Sometimes the difference in start time can be just an hour or two and cause the results to differ because the one that started first will have a few trades that the second does not have.

--- 帖子 #1914 ---
Hi guys,

Yes i agree Pluto2 that this is a very good variation to trade the basket.  Also thanks Caillou for the _suv variant.

Observations:

1/  If a pure hedge has absolutely no DD (other than the locked in hedge loss), the next best basket is the correlated pairs, eg E/U and U/CHF they will produce minimal DD most of the time... then I would suggest that the three pair trade basket would produce the next 'least' amount of DD.  And a full 14 pair basket will be so loose in its basket relationships that it can produce large DD's before rebalancing as we have seen.  As such I think you will get significantly more DD from the six pairs traded on the Addsix EA's than with Caillou's 3 pairs being traded.

2/  My Phantom3_suv closed out twice in the last 24 hours.  DD max about 1.5%.  (I will start to track the results.)  And this was running it through the slow asian sessions also.  It remains to be seen if the three pairs can allow enough equity pops to make the EA viable.  Certainly we could increase the contract size we are trading to compensate.....  I assume there is a relationship between the number of pairs traded and, the standard devaition on the DD curve???  If so - is there an optimal number of pairs to trade in the basket... i guess we will just have to keep testing to find out.  I am happy with the three pairs as the way to go for now.

3/  Trading a reverse version is a sure way to big DD's - since we know that clean trends will occur and these will be very hard for the basket to recover from.  But if we are trading with the trend as we are at present - then we suffer small incremental DD increases while we are in the range and then the eventual trending move will get us to our target pp.  The main difference is that the basket is ideally designed to manage ranges by constantly hedging itself  - and it can do this much more efficiently when price action is ranging.

Tim

Hi Caillou,

Possible additional variable to be added to the Phantom3.30_suv would be to have it only restart a new trade sequence an hour prior to the London open.  If it is still in a trade sequence from the day before it would just continue through the Asian session.  But when it closes out it will wait for the London session to start new sequence.

In this way we would avoid the (usually flat) asian session and so minimise DD further, allowing us to increase our contract size further(?) ... this again would need testing.

I know Sidhujag has built something like this into his series of EA's on the other thread, but they are all six pair trading variants, and I think a simple delay to trade activity in the London session should do the trick.

If you get some time to add this to the EA (as a true/ false variable) I would be grateful

--- 帖子 #1917 ---
I see many people bring up the "perfect hedge" comment, I think we all should read this post I read a while ago:

http://www.forexfactory.com/showpost...&postcount=134

It explains that buying and selling 1 lot is NOT a hedge.  For example:

"SELL 1Lot CHF/JPY means selling CHF 100 K (1 Lot), which is a dept of CHF 100K which buys for your balance JPY 9,883,000 on assets. "

Not sure if this will influence the EA but it should be given some attention.

The idea of the synthetic hedge is exactly that... a synthetic "edge" to help us out when trades mount up.. to avoid margin call.. thats all it is.

--- 帖子 #1924 ---
The other point to be made about the 3 pair trading approach is that it is very efficient on margin used.  There is a possiblity that there are less trades causing a 'drag' on the pair with the momentum (in the positive direction) - so 'in theory' this should mean we will get less margin used to achieve the equity pop.  Since there is a higher chance of more trades that turn negative with more pairs slowing down a close out...ie the more pairs being traded the more 'muddy' the water is  Not sure if this is actually true.

But watching the Phantom3 EA's operate they certainly have incredibly low DD's for the last few days and have shown less than half the DD's of the Addsix series that I had running and have seen from Frazerd etc.

Time and testing will tell I guess.

Tim

--- 帖子 #1926 ---
Not sure about this.  I was thinking more that we could possibly reach the pp quicker because there are less other pairs to conflict with a clean move (in one of the three pairs).  I do not think that it follows that it will get unbalanced quicker also - since the other pairs are equally quick to react  - this is not the case with less aligned pairs in a bigger basket.

I am not sure also about the 30 min trading - BUT - I am certain that the extra trades dynamically make no difference to the three pair trading basket (or any basket for that matter).  It just allows the basket to react to the market conditions quicker (but doesn't make it more efficient or inefficient in terms of the basket itself).  Sure it will add to the margin used - but this is very low anyways.

In theory it shouldn't add to the DD either, since the other pairs have equal chance (every 30 min)to restabilize the basket.  It just allows the trade sequence to be more dynamic and react quicker to the market...I hope I am making myself clear on this.....

Again time will tell.

Tim

--- 帖子 #1937 ---
Just remember that Caillou is using 500:1 leverage. If your leverage is not 500:1 his settings probably will not work for your account. Also, keep in mind that timing (when you enter the market with the new settings) has a lot to do with how well the EA performs the first few days.

As an example, my AddSix_01x is doing great since adding the x factor on my original demo, but I started another account with same EA, same settings, same leverage, same everything except start time. It has been running since 10 Nov and has not closed yet - 66 open trades, 343% lowest margin and -6.3% max DD.

Sometimes you get into a good flow and sometimes you don't. We need to concentrate on figuring out the optimum time to start the EAs. I start most of mine on Sunday evening when the market opens or late at night on other days. Those seem to do better than the few that I open during the daytime. It may be because they catch the London opening early on and not the Asian. That's why I think those who are concentrating on the different market hours may come up with a good solution.

--- 帖子 #1954 ---
You need to think about this.  A tighter reaction will limit the drawdown NOT increase it.  It will increase the margin used (although with only three pairs trading this is much less than other EA series such as the Addsix EA's).

The DD is limited because if the direction of the overall position goes negative it is quickly rebalanced.

Distributing your money across more pairs (with less direct association to each other) means it will take more time and trades to rebalance.  This means that sometimes there will be a bigger DD blow out (but not always).

We saw this clearly with the 14 pair basket trades (Phantom or Basket series), and the newer versions have much less DD.  The three pair basket has less again.

Tim

Hi,

I wanted to be able to do some backtests over a longer period of time without having to wait for months to get results so I converted one of the EAs (AddSix_01x) to MT5.

If anyone is interested here it is.

Results do not look very good so far (Huge drawdowns, Statements included) BUT

- I am not 100 % sure yet everything runs as in MT4

- I am not sure if these "strategy tester" backtests are accurate at all. To be able to tell so I will try to compare the results with my realtime demo tests.  Have to let it run for some weeks in order to have something to compare with.

If you want to try it for yourself make sure

- you have all 14 pairs. I use Alpari MT5 which you can get here: http://www.alpari.co.uk/files/site_u...k_mt5setup.exe

- you have the VOM (Virtual Order Manager) extension which you can get here: http://www.mql5.com/en/articles/88

- you delete the CSV files generated by VOM after each run, else you will get different results each time (didnt figure out why yet)

--- 帖子 #1969 ---
Not only that the time of the bars are not synchronized, go and test for yourself you will see what I mean.

This code should help a bit but it is not a true solution:

void OnTick()

{

string Symbols[3];

Symbols[0] = "EURJPY";

Symbols[1] = "USDJPY";

Symbols[2] = "EURUSD";

int N = 2;

int RoundNum;

ENUM_TIMEFRAMES TimeFrame = _Period;

int i;

datetime dta[1];

static datetime LastBarTime;

// pair 0 (among N) is the "driver"

CopyTime(Symbols[0],TimeFrame,0,1,dta);

if (dta[0] != LastBarTime) {

RoundNum++;

Print("Debug --- Round ",RoundNum);

LastBarTime = dta[0];

for (i=0; i<=N; i++) {

CopyTime(Symbols[i],Period(),0,1,dta);

Print("Debug --- Symbol ",Symbols[i]," : Time ",dta[0]);

}

// Do your stuff here.

Process();

}

}

--- 帖子 #1992 ---
The test results you saw are only the BASIC phantom addsix.  It buys or sells the biggest winner from the two baskets every hour.  The phantoms are reset every x hours.

I will code versions for the AddSix02 and 03 soon just need to figure out what makes them different.

Metatrader 5 is not the same as Metatrader 4.  Metaquotes revamped the entire order handling system.

In MT4 you can have more than one order for a currency pair.  In MT5 you can't.

The term orders is not used anymore, in MT5 you talk about positions.  You can only have ONE position open per currency pair.  But you can add to the existing position.  Think of a basket with eggs.  The basket is the position, the eggs are the orders you placed.  You cannot manage the orders individually only the basket as a whole.

So it is not possible to close the biggest losing order in MT5, what is possible is to close the biggest losing position, but that position includes all orders opened for the currency pair.

Hope you understand what I'm trying to say.

This is actually a good thing for this strategy because MT does not need to close 50 trades and take 5 minutes.  MT5 only has max 6 positions to close which is obviously a lot faster.

But even if it were possible it won't work.  The problem is where do you draw the line?  When do you tell if a order is ready to be closed?  This will change the dynamics of the system to the core and it might not work anymore.

What we are needing is to PREVENT it from happening, not sure if it is even possible.

One idea that I had a while ago is to balance all 6 pairs out in case of an emergency, that is to make a perfect hedge.  This will enable your account to stay alive and wait the storm out.  As soon as the market settles you start to unbalance the hedge again.

This is of course very difficult, linear algebra iterative operations needs to be programmed to find the lots to buy or sell to make a perfect hedge.

--- 帖子 #2012 ---
I, and I think probably several others, use a EA that will close all trades in case of emergencies or it could be used as you suggest as well. However, the EA will close all the trades when equity reaches Equity Profit Target. Equity Profit Target is determined by ProfitPercent (PP), a external input item that the user sets as desired. Most of us set that at .5% and I don't think anyone sets it higher than 1%. That variable can be changed at any time while the EA is running. So, if you have it set at .5 and you have a lot of trades accumulated and want to take less profit to get a basket closed quicker, just reset PP to .1, or if you are willing to accept a small loss to get the basket closed, set it to -.5.

The point is, you don't have to use a Close-All EA to do what you suggest. It can be done using the settings that are already in these EAs. However, if it makes you feel any better, here is a Close-All EA. I keep this EA on all my platforms just in case something goes wrong and I need to get all trades closed quickly.

--- 帖子 #2023 ---
Not true, the init function can be programmed to have a loop that calls the start function at specified intervals. This has a set of side-effects that are not always desirable for regular EAs, but for a close-all EA, it can be most desirable. It requires a degree of sophistication by the user, such as being sure to only run the loop-driven EA as long as needed, then remove it from the chart or close the chart it's attached to.

All further support/answers given...........elsewhere.

Hi, all. First, I am newbie as a trader, but I like programming in C and  C++, so I find easy to code on MQL, and I am learning by now. I am  sorry if my english is not good enough, but I am spanish.

Well, I like the Phantom trading idea, as well as Basket trading. The  problem to me is that we can't backtest it's results and tune up the  system before forward testing it. And I am sure you see as a valuable  tool if you can backtest it.

First, I did try to traslate the EAs coded for MT4, for running into  MT5, but it was a hard an non profitable job, because some functions  doesn't traslate directly and others simply are removed. As you know,  MT5 allows backtest multicurrency EAs, but its Order management is not  as I like (it allows only trade following FIFO management, and not in  visual mode).

Then, I have a good idea: why not backtest on MT4, but reading the rates  of the other currrencies from a file? I am coding an EA that reads the  historical data from a pair and writes three data for every tick:  DateTime, Bid and Ask. Unfortunately, this EA can only work on MT5,  because it's the only one platform that downloads historical data on  every tick and with different Bid and Ask data. The EA can be launched  on backtest, so writing all the historical data from each pair doesn't  spends more than a few minutes.

This is just the first stage. From here, I have two options:

a) Re-code the main EA (Phantom EA, by instance), in the way that every  call to the function MarketInfo(...), changing as another function that  reads the file wrote previously.

b) The more elegant. Create an indicator the reads the files and serves  the data to the main EA. We can, too, show the data in a beautiful way,  as bars or candles.

What do you think about it? Some better ideas? Thanks.
